[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:War)

:   "*A young Jedi named Darth Vader, who was a pupil of mine until he turned to evil, helped the Empire hunt down and destroy the Jedi Knights. He betrayed and murdered your father. Now the Jedi are all but extinct.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to Luke Skywalker[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-12)

The **Great Jedi Purge** ([19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY")—[3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY")), also known as the **war against the Jedi**, was the sixteen [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year")—long genocide that saw the scattered survivors of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") [hunted](/wiki/Jedi_hunter "Jedi hunter") down by the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") after the initial execution of [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), in which [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") [slaughtered](/wiki/Death "Death") the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") upon the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") command. After the Imperial [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius") erased all traces of the Jedi Order they could find from existence, their objective was completed and the Jedi were all but extinct, the Inquisitors themselves seamlessly vanishing as well.

The campaign against the Jedi traced its origins to the [ancient wars](/wiki/Sith_Wars "Sith Wars") between the Jedi and the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"), who were [nearly](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") [eliminated](/wiki/Defeat_of_the_Sith "Defeat of the Sith") around [1032 BBY](/wiki/1032_BBY "1032 BBY"). The Sith in fact continued operating in secret, plotting their [eventual destruction](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan") of the Jedi. A [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") after the defeat of the Sith, [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, using his public persona of [senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") and then [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") Sheev Palpatine, forced [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") into the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars") as a pretext for gaining emergency executive power over the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"). He used the war to manipulate and deceive the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") into giving his office virtually unchecked executive power in the name of security. In addition, the [clone army](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") that provided the Republic with its military force had secretly been implanted with [bio-chips](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") by its Sith creators that, upon activation, would trigger total compliance and force the clones into killing their Jedi leaders.

The Great Jedi Purge began at the end of the Clone Wars. [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") believed to be the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") destined to destroy the Sith, discovered that Palpatine was Darth Sidious and informed [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"). In what Sidious would publicly label the "Jedi rebellion," Windu and three other Masters confronted the Chancellor, who killed the three Masters and engaged Windu in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office"). Skywalker, who sought power from Sidious in order to save his wife, [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), from death, betrayed and incapacitated Windu before the Jedi Master could kill the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord"). Sidious then killed Windu, and Skywalker became the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") Darth Vader and led [Operation: Knightfall](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall"), killing everyone inside the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace"). While Vader carried out the assault, Sidious initiated Order 66, with the latter causing the clones' biochips to brainwash them into betraying and slaughtering the Jedi, ultimately leading to the Jedi Order being destroyed. With the Jedi branded traitors and the Clone Wars at an end, Sidious declared himself [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") and [transformed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the Republic into a Galactic Empire.

The [Age of the Empire](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") saw the continued hunting of the Jedi survivors who were either not involved with the clones or escaped the trap survived and vex the Empire in years after. Vader commanded a number of Inquisitors, that was revealed following the formation of the Empire, whose job was to hunt any Jedi survivors. [The Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"), a former [Jedi Temple Guard](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_Guard "Jedi Temple Guard") from [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"), hunted a group of [rebels](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres") on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal") who were led by a former [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan"), [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"). These rebels ultimately helped create the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"), which fought against the Empire during the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War"). The final act of the purge came [on](/wiki/Mission_to_Malachor "Mission to Malachor") [Malachor](/wiki/Malachor "Malachor"), during which the former Sith Lord [Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul") resurfaced, and Vader dueled his former Padawan, [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano")—who assumed dead allowed the Great Jedi Purge to end.

## Prelude[]

:   "*At last, we will reveal ourselves to the Jedi. At last, we will have revenge.*"
:   ―Darth Maul — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6b/RevengeAtLast-TPM.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250307223813)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:RevengeAtLast-TPM.flac "File:RevengeAtLast-TPM.flac"))[[33]](#cite_note-Episode_I-33)

Many thousands of [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo"), a [rogue Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_rogue_Jedi "Unidentified rogue Jedi") began using the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"), believing that it was the dark side where the true potential of the [powers](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") lied. While this caused him to be expelled from the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"), he gained followers and formed a new order[[34]](#cite_note-Sith-34) that eventually became the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"). Soon, the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") and Sith became bitter enemies and [waged many wars against each other](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War"). Ultimately, the Sith's greed for power led to infighting within their order, which the Jedi took advantage of, defeating and nearly destroying the Sith. Following their victory, the Jedi believed that the Sith were extinct. However, one [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord"), [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane"), survived and plotted his revenge by enacting the [Great Plan](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan")[[35]](#cite_note-HC_2-35) and the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"), which allowed the Sith to operate in secret without anyone, particularly the Jedi, knowing. They would number two at any given time—a [master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") and an [apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice")—and henceforth used cunning and conspiracy rather than brute force to carry out their plans to destroy the Jedi Order and eventually rise again to subjugate [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").[[36]](#cite_note-Bane_Databank-36)

The Sith operated in secret for [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century"). In the years before the Invasion of Naboo, [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") became the apprentice of [Darth Plagueis](/wiki/Darth_Plagueis "Darth Plagueis") and took on the name Darth Sidious. As a Sith, Sidious betrayed and killed his master and became a [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith"). In his public persona of [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") Palpatine of Naboo, Sidious carried out his plans to gain power over the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"). He planned to deceive and destroy the Jedi and Republic, then usher in a Sith dominion over the galaxy, with himself as sovereign ruler over an empire that would allow him to cast the galaxy into darkness and unlock the ancient secrets of the Sith and the dark side of the Force. In doing so, Sidious believed he could remake the universe in his own designs.[[37]](#cite_note-Tarkin-37) Infiltrating the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), Republic and Jedi, allowed him to carry out his plans.

 [![After a thousand years in hiding, the Sith revealed themselves to the Jedi during the final years of the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/DotF_TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20240522042217) [![After a thousand years in hiding, the Sith revealed themselves to the Jedi during the final years of the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/DotF_TPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240522042217)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/DotF_TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20240522042217) 

After a thousand years in hiding, the Sith revealed themselves to the Jedi during the final years of the Galactic Republic.

 

Sidious orchestrated the Invasion of Naboo, in which the Sith—through his apprentice, [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), before Maul was defeated—revealed themselves to the Jedi, as a means of gaining power. As Senator Palpatine, he manipulated and deceived Naboo's ruler, [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), to call for a [Vote of No Confidence](/wiki/Vote_of_No_Confidence "Vote of No Confidence") in the leadership of [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum"). Palpatine was nominated to succeed Valorum and ultimately won the election, placing him in charge of the Republic.[[33]](#cite_note-Episode_I-33) Around the same time, [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas"), a member of the [Jedi Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") who believed that a galactic war was imminent, secretly ordered the creation of a [clone army](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") on [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino"). Sifo-Dyas, who was killed at the behest of fallen Jedi Master [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), who became Sidious' apprentice after Maul was assumed dead on Naboo, intended the army to be used for the Republic.[[38]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-38) Dooku, as Darth Tyranus, secretly took over the project, and the Sith saw to it that [bio-chips](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") were added to each clone trooper. These chips contained [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66"), a command that when executed, would forcibly brainwash the clone troopers into believing that the Jedi were traitors to the Republic that needed to be executed, causing the clones to execute the Jedi.[[39]](#cite_note-Fugitive-39)

The years that followed the Naboo Crisis saw the advent of the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"), in which thousands of [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") seceded from the Republic and joined the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). This period of political tension and the calls for war were orchestrated by the Sith, as a means for Sidious to gain further control over the galaxy. In order to allow for Chancellor Palpatine to adopt the clone army to respond to what the Republic saw as the threat of the Separatist Alliance, [Junior Representative](/wiki/Junior_Representative "Junior Representative") [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks") of Naboo called on the Galactic Senate to give the Chancellor emergency executive power. The Senate granted the Chancellor the power, the clone army was commissioned as the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"), and the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars") began shortly thereafter during the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis").[[40]](#cite_note-Episode_II-40) Due to his double identity, Sidious would be able to control the war on both ends and deceive both sides.

 [![Grand Master Yoda beheld the impending Jedi Purge through a Force vision.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Yoda_vision_of_the_Jedi_Purge.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224055921) [![Grand Master Yoda beheld the impending Jedi Purge through a Force vision.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Yoda_vision_of_the_Jedi_Purge.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200224055921)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/49/Yoda_vision_of_the_Jedi_Purge.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224055921) 

Grand Master Yoda beheld the impending Jedi Purge through a Force vision.

 

The Jedi Order was placed in charge of the war effort, with Jedi serving as [Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") and [Commanders](/wiki/Commander "Commander") in the military. After several years of war, many of the galaxy's citizens turned against the conflict and blamed the Jedi leaders for the prolonged and devastating war. Public opinion, therefore, began to turn against the Jedi, with many in the public viewing the Jedi Order as synonymous with the Clone Wars.[[41]](#cite_note-Sabotage-41) [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee"), a member of the Order, also viewed the Jedi as having become complicit in a mistaken war, leading her to [bomb](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar") the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant").[[42]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-42) Other Jedi also shared her views; Jedi Master [Depa Billaba](/wiki/Depa_Billaba "Depa Billaba") believed it was a mistake for the Jedi to lead the Clone Wars.[[43]](#cite_note-Kanan_1-43) [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"), after setting out on a spiritual path to learn the secrets of [eternal consciousness](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") within the Force, saw a [vision](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision") on [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah") of Jedi fighting clone troopers and being killed by Darth Sidious.[[44]](#cite_note-Voices-44) Through his journey, he came to believe that the Jedi Order may have lost the Clone Wars simply by fighting in it. He suspected that the Jedi would lose the war, but ultimately be victorious in the fight against the Sith.[[45]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-45)

At some point during the Clone Wars, the Jedi Master [Eno Cordova](/wiki/Eno_Cordova "Eno Cordova") entered the Zeffo vault on Bogano and experienced a vision depicting the Jedi's destruction and the subsequent spread of the Dark Side across the galaxy. He thus raced back to Coruscant and presented his findings to the Jedi Council, only to be met with skepticism and disbelief. The only one who seemed to put faith in his vision was his old confidant Jocasta Nu. Nu subsequently entrusted into Cordova's care a [holocron](/wiki/Eno_Cordova%27s_holocron "Eno Cordova's holocron") containing a secret list of youngling Force sensitives across the galaxy.[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1)

Towards the end of the war, the clone conspiracy was nearly uncovered when clone trooper [Tup](/wiki/Tup "Tup") suffered from a premature activation of Order 66. He betrayed and murdered Jedi Master [Tiplar](/wiki/Tiplar "Tiplar") during the [Battle of Ringo Vinda](/wiki/Battle_of_Ringo_Vinda "Battle of Ringo Vinda").[[46]](#cite_note-The_Unknown-46) After Tup's death, his friend and fellow trooper, [Fives](/wiki/Fives "Fives"), investigated what happened and learned about the bio-chip and the Order 66 conspiracy. He confronted the Chancellor, who revealed his involvement before staging an assassination attempt against himself for which Fives was framed. Fives told two of his commanders, Jedi [General](/wiki/General "General") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), a [Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") of the Jedi Order[[47]](#cite_note-Orders-47) who was believed to be the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"),[[33]](#cite_note-Episode_I-33) and [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Rex](/wiki/Rex "Rex"), about the conspiracy, but they did not believe him. Fives was killed by a fellow clone after being viewed as a threat, and the official story of what happened to Tup was that he was exposed to a parasite that made him violent.[[47]](#cite_note-Orders-47) The Jedi later learned that the Sith were involved in the creation of the clone army, but they did not learn of the conspiracy and continued to use the clones as their only means of combating the Separatist Alliance.[[38]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-38)

## The Jedi Purge[]

### The "Jedi rebellion"[]

:   "*In the name of the Galactic Senate of the Republic, you're under arrest, Chancellor.*"  
    "*Are you threatening me, Master Jedi?*"
:   ―Mace Windu and Sheev Palpatine[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5)

The final days of the Clone Wars saw Chancellor Palpatine amassing more central authority, and the Jedi Council becoming increasingly distrustful of the Chancellor and his growing power. They felt that the dark side of the Force surrounded the Chancellor, though they did not yet know that he was the Dark Lord they had been searching for the entire war. The [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant") which was orchestrated by Sidious, saw Dooku being betrayed by Sidious, and then killed by Anakin at the behest of Palpatine. With Dooku dead, the Chancellor promised a swift end to the war once General [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"), the leader of the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"), was killed. The Jedi Council, wary of the Chancellor's claims that he would give up his executive power, privately discussed removing the Chancellor from office if he did not give up his power upon Grievous' death.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5)

It was in the war's last days when Anakin Skywalker began having visions of his wife, now-Senator Amidala, dying in [childbirth](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction"). Determined to save his wife and their unborn child—the couple was unaware that they were expecting [twins](/wiki/Twin "Twin")—Skywalker began searching for the power to save his family. Palpatine regaled him with the [Tragedy of Darth Plagueis the Wise](/wiki/Tragedy_of_Darth_Plagueis_the_Wise "Tragedy of Darth Plagueis the Wise"), which he described as an old Sith legend, and explained that Plagueis was a Dark Lord of the Sith who had unlocked the secrets of [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality"). Shortly thereafter, the Chancellor revealed to the errant Jedi Knight that he was indeed Darth Sidious and that he could help Skywalker save Amidala's life. Skywalker initially rejected the opportunity and informed Jedi Master [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), a member of the Jedi Council, about the Chancellor's identity and deception.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5)

 [![The confrontation in the Chancellor's office sparked the beginning of the Great Jedi Purge.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/14/Anakin-Makes-A-Choice.png/revision/latest?cb=20210516171122) [![The confrontation in the Chancellor's office sparked the beginning of the Great Jedi Purge.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/14/Anakin-Makes-A-Choice.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/270?cb=20210516171122)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/14/Anakin-Makes-A-Choice.png/revision/latest?cb=20210516171122) 

The confrontation in the Chancellor's office sparked the beginning of the Great Jedi Purge.

 

Knowing the Chancellor's deception and true identity, and with Palpatine having not yet given up his executive power despite the death of General Grievous during the [Battle of Utapau](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau"), Windu assembled a team of three other Jedi Masters—[Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto"), [Agen Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar "Agen Kolar"), and [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin")—to arrest the Chancellor and stop his plans. The Jedi Masters [confronted](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") the Chancellor in his office, and Sidious lashed out at them, killing the three other Jedi Masters and engaging Windu in a lightsaber duel. The duel moved throughout the Chancellor's office until Windu disarmed the Dark Lord, at which point Skywalker arrived to witness what Sidious claimed was the Jedi trying to take over the Republic. Because he needed Sidious to survive in order to save Amidala's life, Skywalker betrayed Windu by cutting off his hand, before Windu could kill Sidious. Sidious used the opportunity to unleash a torrent of [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") on the Jedi Master, sending Windu out the window and to his death. Having betrayed and turned against the Jedi Order, Skywalker pledged himself to Darth Sidious and became the Sith Lord known as Darth Vader.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5)

### Fall of the Jedi[]

#### Across the stars[]

:   "*This is Master Obi-Wan Kenobi. I regret to report that both our Jedi Order and the Republic have fallen, with the dark shadow of the Empire rising to take their place. This message is a warning and a reminder for any surviving Jedi: trust in the Force. Do* not *return to the Temple. That time has passed, and our future is uncertain.* Avoid Coruscant*. Avoid detection. Be* secret*—but be* strong*. We will each be challenged: our trust, our faith, our friendships. But we must persevere and, in time, I believe* a new hope *will emerge. May the Force be with you always.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi, to all surviving Jedi[[17]](#cite_note-Kanan_2-17)

 [![On the orders of Darth Sidious, Darth Vader and the 501st Legion marched on the Jedi Temple.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/Knightfall2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208032337) [![On the orders of Darth Sidious, Darth Vader and the 501st Legion marched on the Jedi Temple.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/Knightfall2.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130208032337)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/Knightfall2.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208032337) 

On the orders of Darth Sidious, Darth Vader and the 501st Legion marched on the Jedi Temple.

 

Windu's attempt on Sidious' life gave the Dark Lord the justification he needed to brand the Jedi as [traitors](/wiki/Treason "Treason") and destroy the Jedi Order. He ordered Vader to go to the Jedi Temple and kill every Jedi who was inside, and then [execute the Separatist Council](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar"). Vader brought with him a battalion of clone troopers, ones loyal to the Sith as a result of Sidious' activation of Protocol 66. While Vader and the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion") participated in [Operation: Knightfall](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall"), Sidious ordered clone commanders across the galaxy to begin executing Order 66. With Sidious issuing order 66, the bio-chips activated and then brainwashed the clones into believing that the Jedi were traitors to the Republic that needed to be executed. On worlds such as [Mygeeto](/wiki/Mygeeto "Mygeeto"), [Felucia](/wiki/Felucia "Felucia"), [Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Cato_Neimoidia "Cato Neimoidia"), [Saleucami](/wiki/Saleucami "Saleucami"),[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) and [Kaller](/wiki/Kaller "Kaller"),[[17]](#cite_note-Kanan_2-17) clone forces killed their Jedi commanders. The Jedi were caught off-guard by their clone troopers' sudden betrayal. Some Jedi, including Jedi Master [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") on [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"), Master [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli") and [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") Yoda on [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"),[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) Padawan [Caleb Dume](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") on Kaller,[[17]](#cite_note-Kanan_2-17) Padawan [Cal Kestis](/wiki/Cal_Kestis "Cal Kestis") over [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca"),[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1) former Padawan [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") [aboard](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Tribunal "Skirmish aboard the Tribunal")[[15]](#cite_note-Shattered-15) the *[Tribunal](/wiki/Tribunal "Tribunal")*,[[48]](#cite_note-TCW_Character_Encyclopedia-48) and [Grogu](/wiki/Din_Grogu "Din Grogu") on Coruscant,[[49]](#cite_note-The_Mandalorian:_Chapter_13-49) managed to escape.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5)

Surprisingly, not every Jedi was marked for immediate execution. Certain Jedi, such as Jedi Knight [Iskat Akaris](/wiki/Thirteenth_Sister "Thirteenth Sister"), were spared from the immediate onslaught of Order 66. Some Jedi who held doubts in the Jedi Order were watched and influenced by spies placed in the Jedi Temple by Darth Sidious. Their goal was to encourage and grow doubts and disillusion in the Order within these troubled Jedi, making them more susceptible to the idea of leaving the Order or embracing the Dark side. When the order came and the purge began, these Jedi were spared from the onslaught. The clones who normally should have raised blasters, instead raised a hologram of Sidious himself to them, who offered them a chance to live, as long as they revoked their Jedi ways and pledged their allegiance to him. These Jedi would soon become the first [Inquisitors](/wiki/Inquisitor "Inquisitor") of the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius").[[20]](#cite_note-Inquisitor:_Rise_of_the_Red_Blade-20)

Nevertheless, most Jedi died. This included in the Jedi Temple, where almost everyone, including [younglings](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling"), were killed by Vader and his clone forces. Hoping to lure more Jedi to their deaths, Vader activated a [beacon](/wiki/Jedi_beacon "Jedi beacon") inside the Jedi Temple that broadcast an emergency message requesting all Jedi to return to the Temple.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) Around the time of Order 66, Master [Tobar Ka-Teen](/wiki/Tobar_Ka-Teen "Tobar Ka-Teen") was presumed to have been killed on [Auratera](/wiki/Auratera "Auratera") by several [squads](/wiki/Squad "Squad") of clone troopers.[[50]](#cite_note-Nexus-50) In what would be remembered as the [last stand of the Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_survivors%27_last_stand "Jedi survivors' last stand"), one group of survivors took up a defensive position within a [mountain](/wiki/Mountain "Mountain") [fortress](/wiki/Fortress "Fortress"), which was attacked by Republic clone troopers. Reportedly it was the [Republic officer](/wiki/Republic_officer "Republic officer") [Hodnar Borrum](/wiki/Hodnar_Borrum "Hodnar Borrum") who marshaled the clones for the final charge, which ended with the defeat of the Jedi. That battle may have been fought on Madar or Morad.[[19]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-19)

#### Palpatine's empire is born[]

:   "*Emperor* Palpatine *rose to power because he made people afraid. He made people fear the* Jedi*. He called them* traitors*. He said they used their mystical powers to subvert democracy and peace, to cause war. It worked, possibly because as much as people* loved *the Jedi, they also* hated *them, on some level. It is hard to look at people who have become their* best selves*. It reminds you that* you have not*.*"
:   ―[The Archivist](/wiki/The_Archivist "The Archivist")[[51]](#cite_note-CrimsonReign3-51)

With the Jedi Order effectively destroyed, Sidious called a special session of the Senate in order to mark the end of the Galactic Republic. The Sith Lord presented himself as a brutally wounded victim of an attempted Jedi coup that he referred to as the "Jedi rebellion." He pledged that the remaining Jedi traitors would be eliminated. He further used the instability wrought by the Clone Wars to [transform](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the Republic into the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), a proclamation that was met with enthusiastic congressional support. After his attack on the temple, Vader proceeded to [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") to eliminate the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council"). Earlier, Sidious had deceived the Council into believing that Vader would protect them. Vader slaughtered the council upon his arrival, which was then followed by him following Sidious's third order by shutting down the Droid army, thus ending the war.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5)

With Palpatine's speech having squarely leveled the blame for recent galactic matters on the Jedi,[[52]](#cite_note-Launchpad229-52) the Jedi, to the galaxy at large, were labeled as warmongers[[51]](#cite_note-CrimsonReign3-51) who had tried to claim the Republic for themselves at the close of a war[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) they had supposedly caused;[[51]](#cite_note-CrimsonReign3-51) the Empire claimed that the Jedi had been behind the Separatist Alliance[[53]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-53) and had been working to subvert the Republic from within.[[51]](#cite_note-CrimsonReign3-51) That Dooku was publicly known to have been a Jedi and then became leader of the Separatist Alliance did little to help the Order's public image.[[54]](#cite_note-Propaganda-54) Further, the peoples of the galaxy were weary of war and thus were open to the idea of the Empire, even if only because it meant an end to the suffering and fighting.[[55]](#cite_note-Outlaws-55)

### Birth of the Empire[]

#### Rise of Darth Vader[]

:   "*At last, the Jedi are no more.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Yoda[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5)

While Sidious proclaimed himself [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") of the galaxy, Kenobi and Yoda [infiltrated](/wiki/Infiltration_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Infiltration of the Jedi Temple") the Jedi Temple and found the destruction left in Vader's wake. Kenobi altered the Jedi beacon to warn the Jedi to avoid Coruscant, and soon saw a [holographic](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram") recording that showed him the truth: Darth Vader, the man responsible for the deaths in the Jedi Temple, was his former apprentice Anakin Skywalker, as well as that the Chancellor is Sidious and Vader's master. The two Jedi resolved to destroy the Sith, with Yoda confronting the [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor") while Kenobi would track down and kill his former friend.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) Kenobi's message managed to save an undetermined number of Jedi survivors[[56]](#cite_note-TSWB-56) and made it to Dume just as he entered the [Coruscant system](/wiki/Coruscant_system "Coruscant system").[[17]](#cite_note-Kanan_2-17) After a brief [skirmish](/wiki/Ambush_in_the_Coruscant_system "Ambush in the Coruscant system") against a group of [ARC-170s](/wiki/Aggressive_ReConnaissance-170_starfighter "Aggressive ReConnaissance-170 starfighter"), Dume escaped back to Kaller.[[57]](#cite_note-Kanan_3-57)

 [![Obi-Wan Kenobi claims the high ground in his duel with Darth Vader](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Acme-HighGround.png/revision/latest?cb=20250220143751) [![Obi-Wan Kenobi claims the high ground in his duel with Darth Vader](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Acme-HighGround.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250220143751)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Acme-HighGround.png/revision/latest?cb=20250220143751) 

Obi-Wan Kenobi claims the high ground in his duel with Darth Vader

 

Kenobi tracked Vader to the [volcanic](/wiki/Volcano "Volcano") world of Mustafar by stowing away aboard Amidala's ship, after the senator chose to travel to Mustafar in search of her husband. Vader, who slaughtered the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") on Mustafar and brought an end of the Clone Wars, became enraged when he saw his former master, believing that he and Amidala were conspiring against him. Vader attacked Amidala and left her unconscious, while he and Kenobi engaged in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Duel_on_Mustafar "Duel on Mustafar") throughout the Separatist complex and above the lava rivers. Yoda, meanwhile, confronted the Emperor and also [engaged](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Galactic_Senate "Duel in the Galactic Senate") him in a lightsaber duel. While neither conquered the other, Yoda ultimately fled after being unable to defeat the Emperor and was rescued by Senator [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"), the latter being an ally of the Jedi Order. On Mustafar, Kenobi cut off three of Vader's limbs and left the Sith Lord to burn to death on the banks of a lava river, while Kenobi rescued Amidala and left Mustafar. The Emperor soon arrived on Mustafar and found his battered apprentice. They returned to Coruscant, where Vader was given a [suit of life-supporting armor](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_armor "Darth Vader's armor") that he would be forced to wear for the rest of his life.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5)

Kenobi rendezvoused with Yoda and Organa on the [asteroid](/wiki/Asteroid "Asteroid") colony of [Polis Massa](/wiki/Polis_Massa "Polis Massa"), where Amidala gave birth to her twins, [Luke](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") and [Leia](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), before dying. The Jedi Masters knew that if they had any hope of ever defeating the Sith, they would need to keep Anakin's children hidden and safe. Leia was taken to Alderaan, where she was raised by Organa and his wife, [Queen](/wiki/Alderaanian_monarchy "Alderaanian monarchy") [Breha Organa](/wiki/Breha_Organa "Breha Organa"), as [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") Leia Organa. Luke was taken to live with Anakin's stepbrother, [Owen Lars](/wiki/Owen_Lars "Owen Lars"), and Owen's wife, [Beru](/wiki/Beru_Whitesun_Lars "Beru Whitesun Lars"), on [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine"). Kenobi went into exile on Tatooine to watch over the boy, while Yoda returned to Dagobah in seclusion.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5)

In the immediate aftermath of Order 66 and on the steps of the Jedi Temple, the Imperial [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier"), [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda"), led a [public rally](/wiki/Celebration_marking_the_eradication_of_the_Jedi_Order "Celebration marking the eradication of the Jedi Order") celebrating the extermination of the Jedi. Amedda stated that the galactic population was now free from the supposed threat of the Jedi thanks to the new Galactic Emperor. He further claimed that the Jedi had been responsible for Separatist plots and told numerous lies, but that Palpatine had seen through these supposed ploys and survived their assassination attempt. The main event was the incineration of a number of lightsabers, taken from the dead Force-sensitives. The Imperials had also recovered Yoda's lightsaber, with Amedda personally throwing the hilt into the furnace. The [Kyber crystals](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal") in the lightsabers soon reacted to the heat, exploding into a blast of blue light that pushed Amedda and several clones back.[[53]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-53)

#### Darth Vader's first hunts[]

 [![The Inquisitorius was comprised of fallen Jedi who turned to the dark side as a result of the Great Jedi Purge.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/Inquisitors-SWCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20251021051154) [![The Inquisitorius was comprised of fallen Jedi who turned to the dark side as a result of the Great Jedi Purge.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/Inquisitors-SWCT.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20251021051154)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/22/Inquisitors-SWCT.png/revision/latest?cb=20251021051154) 

The Inquisitorius was comprised of fallen Jedi who turned to the dark side as a result of the Great Jedi Purge.

 

The [Age of the Empire](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") saw the continued hunting of Jedi survivors across the galaxy as part of the Empire's effort to exterminate Force-users who did not stand with it.[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1) Darth Vader, ordered by his master to retrieve a new Kyber crystal for a lightsaber to replace the blade lost on Mustafar, [traveled](/wiki/Mission_to_Al%27doleem "Mission to Al'doleem") to the site of a sacred Jedi monastery on the river moon of Al'doleem. There he faced Jedi Master [Kirak Infil'a](/wiki/Kirak_Infil%27a "Kirak Infil'a") and despite losing in their first duel and taking massive damage[[58]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_3-58) he defeated him and took [his lightsaber](/wiki/Kirak_Infil%27a%27s_lightsaber "Kirak Infil'a's lightsaber") as his own.[[59]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_4-59)

In order to hunt them down and eliminate them, the Emperor ordered Vader to train a group called the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius") made up of former Jedi. Their past as Jedi meant the Inquisitors were weak in the dark side of the Force and defensive, unused to attacking. Vader noticed this when he began training them and decided to train them in a purely offensive style. Vader tasked the Grand Inquisitor with studying the records of the Jedi Order to familiarize himself with their enemies and hunt them more efficiently. The Inquisitors were given a hit list of Jedi unaccounted for after the purge including Jedi such as Yoda, Quinlan Vos, Ahsoka Tano and Jocasta Nu.[[18]](#cite_note-Dying_Light_I-18)

Nu, the former Chief Librarian of the Jedi Order, was given special importance. She was attempting to preserve the order by creating a new [hidden school](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu%27s_cache "Jocasta Nu's cache") alongside her assistant [Gar](/wiki/Gar_(human) "Gar (human)"). To do this she needed students and in pursuit of this goal she used a secret tunnel back in to the temple to find a holocron with a list of every Force-sensitive child catalogued prior to Order 66.[[18]](#cite_note-Dying_Light_I-18) While she successfully sneaked in to the temple and retrieved the holocron from a secret vault, her escape was not so easy. While escaping she saw the Grand Inquisitor reading and discarding her books which sent her into a frenzy causing her to attack him.[[60]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_8-60)

 [![Jocasta Nu stands before Darth Vader and clone troopers of the Coruscant Guard.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/VaderHuntsForJocastaNu-2017DarthVader10.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180430062442) [![Jocasta Nu stands before Darth Vader and clone troopers of the Coruscant Guard.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/VaderHuntsForJocastaNu-2017DarthVader10.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20180430062442)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c8/VaderHuntsForJocastaNu-2017DarthVader10.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180430062442) 

Jocasta Nu stands before Darth Vader and clone troopers of the Coruscant Guard.

 

After a brief lightsaber duel against the Grand Inquisitor, she was bested, and only Vader's intervention saved her life. Vader demanded she be taken alive causing an argument between him and the Inquisitor which allowed Nu to escape. She retreated to a computer access room in the Library retrieving a [special weapon](/wiki/Lightsaber_rifle "Lightsaber rifle") and initiating the deletion of the archive files.[[61]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_9-61) After failing to kill him with the weapon and ruining her lightsaber in the process, Nu attempted to kill Vader by self-destructing it, but he redirected it so that it blew a hole in the Temple's outer wall. Grabbing a green-bladed lightsaber from a shelf, Nu took the opportunity to escape out the gap, but was forced to fight off several [Coruscant Guard](/wiki/Coruscant_Guard "Coruscant Guard") shock troopers led by Commander Fox, who also fired on Vader by mistake due to Fox neglecting to provide a description of the Sith Lord.[[62]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_10-62)

Snapping the clone commander's neck, Vader ordered the troopers to take Nu alive, stopping her with the Force after she attempted to commit suicide in order to deny them the information she held. Restrained and confined aboard a patrol transport, Nu was forced to watch as Vader accessed the coveted information: the Kyber memory crystal, containing a list of all known Force-sensitive children in the galaxy. When Nu inquired what her fate would be, Vader ignited his lightsaber but met no resistance from Nu, who accepted her death. The list of names was then destroyed by Vader, to ensure that his master could not use it to find and train other Sith apprentices.[[62]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_10-62)

#### Executions continue on[]

:   "*What Empire?"  
    "THE Empire. The one bent on exterminating Force-sensitives so no one can stand against it?*"
:   ―The Nightsister Merrin and the Jedi Padawan Cal Kestis[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1)

 [![Along with Barriss Offee, the Fourth Sister faced a Jedi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ed/LynJediDuel-Realization.png/revision/latest?cb=20240516044757) [![Along with Barriss Offee, the Fourth Sister faced a Jedi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ed/LynJediDuel-Realization.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240516044757)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ed/LynJediDuel-Realization.png/revision/latest?cb=20240516044757) 

Along with Barriss Offee, the Fourth Sister faced a Jedi.

 

The Grand Inquisitor sent the [Fourth Sister](/wiki/Fourth_Sister "Fourth Sister") and [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee") to eliminate a [Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_human_Jedi "Unidentified human Jedi") working with a rebel cell. Although the Jedi was injured and left for dead by the Fourth Sister, Offee betrayed the Inquisitor after her colleague's actions made her realize the true nature of the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius"). After identifying herself again as a Jedi, which she told Fourth Sister, Offee pushed the Inquisitor off the mountain they were on with the Force and returned to save the Jedi.[[63]](#cite_note-63)

The hunt for Jedi resulted in the capture and eventual death of [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") Luminara Unduli in the [Spire](/wiki/Spire_(Stygeon_Prime) "Spire (Stygeon Prime)"), a heavily fortified former Separatist prison on [Stygeon Prime](/wiki/Stygeon_Prime "Stygeon Prime"). Her bones were kept as they still contained traces of her Force signature even after her death and could lure other Jedi survivors to their deaths by making them believe that she was still alive. This strategy proved effective, with Jedi survivors such as Caleb Dume making for Stygeon Prime only to be caught in a trap.[[7]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Old_Masters-7) The Empire also offered rewards to those who turned in Jedi survivors.[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1) Regardless of whether he was alive or dead, a Jedi yielded a high reward.[[64]](#cite_note-Friends-64)

Order 66 remained in effect throughout Imperial rule, with it being ordered that any suspected or known Jedi had to be shot on sight.[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_5-65) Order 66 subsection [Codicil Nine](/wiki/Codicil_Nine "Codicil Nine") made it illegal to keep Sith artifacts.[[66]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_3-66) During the Purge, Vader personally contacted the clone [Bly](/wiki/Bly "Bly") to help him capture two rebellious Padawans. Vader selected Bly due to his experience with the two Padawans in question, which made him the ideal candidate for the task. Vader and Bly were ultimately successful in killing the Jedi.[[67]](#cite_note-Grand_Army_Encyclopedia-67) One [Jedi](/wiki/Jod_Na_Nawood%27s_master "Jod Na Nawood's master") on the run after Order 66[[68]](#cite_note-SkeletonEW-68) encountered a young [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") named [Jod Na Nawood](/wiki/Jod_Na_Nawood "Jod Na Nawood"), whom she began to train before she was found and killed. Nawood was forced to watch his mentor's execution and was left with a bitter outlook on life.[[69]](#cite_note-SC6-69)

Having escaped execution on Kaller and above Coruscant, Dume continued to run from the Empire and joined the [crew](/wiki/Janus_Kasmir%27s_crew "Janus Kasmir's crew") of [smuggler](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler") [Janus Kasmir](/wiki/Janus_Kasmir "Janus Kasmir"). The two managed to escape [clone trooper officers](/wiki/Clone_trooper_officer "Clone trooper officer") [Grey](/wiki/Grey_(clone_trooper) "Grey (clone trooper)") and [Styles](/wiki/Styles "Styles") by leaving each of their smuggling jobs right away after getting paid. However, they were finally caught on the planet [Lahn](/wiki/Lahn "Lahn"),[[70]](#cite_note-Kanan_4-70) only for Styles to take Dume in alive so he could enjoy executing the Padawan who had caused them so much trouble, much to the anger of Grey who simply wanted the supposed traitor dead. As their [*Gozanti*-class cruiser](/wiki/Grey_and_Styles%27_Gozanti-class_cruiser "Grey and Styles' Gozanti-class cruiser") entered the [Kaller system](/wiki/Kaller_system "Kaller system"), Dume managed to break Grey out of the trance of Order 66 by reminding him of his friendship with Master Billaba. After Dume [escaped](/wiki/Rescue_of_Caleb_Dume "Rescue of Caleb Dume") out the [airlock](/wiki/Airlock "Airlock") to join Kasmir and his other allies in a battle against the clones' [cruiser](/wiki/Cruiser "Cruiser"), Grey gave his own life to ensure the Padawan escaped by destroying his ship's controls, leaving the Gozanti to explode with him and Styles aboard.[[71]](#cite_note-Kanan_5-71)

### Establishing the Empire's Perpetual Enemy[]

While Palpatine was content to allow the Imperial military to secure the Empire by whatever means necessary, Palpatine was nonetheless cognizant of the specific threat that the Jedi could still pose. In addition to Vader and the Inquisitorius, Palpatine mobilized military and propaganda efforts against the elusive "Jedi menace", crafting a narrative that would reframe the Jedi from its heroic image during the Clone Wars[[72]](#cite_note-RiseFall-72)—an image that had already been tarnished by the war's prolonged nature,[[41]](#cite_note-Sabotage-41) its outbreak in the first place, the Order's focus on waging it instead of acting as peacekeepers,[[73]](#cite_note-Who_Knew_Too_Much-73)[[74]](#cite_note-Trace-74) and the initial wave of anti-Jedi propaganda that claimed they had been behind the Confederacy[[53]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_1-53)—to a treasonous force that was simultaneously weak and strong at the same time.[[72]](#cite_note-RiseFall-72)

As part of its efforts, the [Imperial Security Bureau](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") and [Commission for the Preservation of the New Order](/wiki/Commission_for_the_Preservation_of_the_New_Order "Commission for the Preservation of the New Order") immediately deleted and blocked all references to teaching curriculum that the Galactic Republic had taught in regards to the beneficial role of the Jedi Order in its society. The ISB coordinated efforts with [Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") Dreshilav to display an implied threat of brutality towards any who showed sympathies to the Jedi, resulting in the destruction of toys in many homes within the [Recopi system](/wiki/Recopi_system "Recopi system") aiding in scrubbing the memory of the Jedi from the children who used to celebrate and look up to them. On certain worlds where streets, statues and buildings had been named after the Jedi, actions were taken to tear them down and/or rename them. A few local governors and Moffs took the extra initiative to remake the statues' rubble into statues in honor of Palpatine instead.[[72]](#cite_note-RiseFall-72)

### Early resistance[]

##### Uprisings on Mon Cala and Raada[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Invasion of Mon Cala](/wiki/Invasion_of_Mon_Cala "Invasion of Mon Cala"), [Raada Uprising](/wiki/Raada_Uprising "Raada Uprising") and [Attack on a farm village](/wiki/Attack_on_a_farm_village "Attack on a farm village")

:   "*Execute Order 66.*""*Don't you* dare*, you stupid* clones*! We're* Inquisitors*, not—*"
:   ―Ferren Barr and the Tenth Brother, as the former tricked nearby Purge Troopers to turn against the Inquisitors[[75]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_17-75)

 [![Darth Vader dueled Ferren Barr on Mon Cala.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/BarrVSVader-2017DarthVader17.png/revision/latest?cb=20180619234627) [![Darth Vader dueled Ferren Barr on Mon Cala.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/BarrVSVader-2017DarthVader17.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180619234627)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/BarrVSVader-2017DarthVader17.png/revision/latest?cb=20180619234627) 

Darth Vader dueled Ferren Barr on Mon Cala.

 

By [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"),[[76]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_16_date-76) former Padawan [Ferren Barr](/wiki/Ferren_Barr "Ferren Barr")[[77]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_16-77) had begun influencing [king](/wiki/King_of_Mon_Cala "King of Mon Cala") [Lee-Char](/wiki/Lee-Char "Lee-Char") of [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala") into open rebellion against the Empire. In retaliation to this, the Emperor sent Vader, along with three Inquisitors, [Tenth Brother](/wiki/Tenth_Brother "Tenth Brother"), [Ninth Sister](/wiki/Ninth_Sister "Ninth Sister"), and [Sixth Brother](/wiki/Sixth_Brother "Sixth Brother"), to the water world to learn the truth about what was happening on Mon Cala and if Jedi were present, then Vader was to destroy them.[[21]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_13-21) During the ensuing [conflict](/wiki/Invasion_of_Mon_Cala "Invasion of Mon Cala"), Vader captured Lee-Char and killed Ferren Barr, but Barr's acolyte [Verla](/wiki/Verla "Verla") escaped after he told her to find another surviving Jedi such as [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos") or Yoda to finish her training.[[75]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_17-75)

In the same year,[[78]](#cite_note-Ahsoka_novel_date-78) the Sixth Brother was sent to [Thabeska](/wiki/Thabeska "Thabeska") to hunt for a possible Force-sensitive. Unbeknownst to him, this is where Tano had been in hiding. After discovering the Inquisitor's presence, Ahsoka fled to [Raada](/wiki/Raada "Raada") and eventually started an early rebel [movement](/wiki/Raada_resistance "Raada resistance"). During the [Raada Uprising](/wiki/Raada_Uprising "Raada Uprising"), she fought the Sixth Brother. She used the Force to cause the Inquisitor's lightsaber to explode, killing him. She later used the now-purified kyber crystals from his saber to build [her own lightsabers](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano%27s_white_lightsabers "Ahsoka Tano's white lightsabers").[[22]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-22) Later, while living within a [farm village](/wiki/Unidentified_farm_village "Unidentified farm village"), Tano [encountered](/wiki/Attack_on_a_farm_village "Attack on a farm village") the [Eleventh Brother](/wiki/Eleventh_Brother "Eleventh Brother") but quickly dispatched him.[[23]](#cite_note-Resolve-23)

##### Hunt for Grandea[]

Former Jedi Knight [Grandea](/wiki/Grandea "Grandea") was spotted in Daiyu, prompting the Ninth Sister and Thirteenth Sister to hunt her down, led by Darth Vader. Grandea was nearly killed, but was able to escape by using a [mind trick](/wiki/Mind_trick "Mind trick") to convince the Inquisitors that they had killed her. The two then reported her death to Vader. Despite surviving, Grandea's right leg was lost, as well as sustaining a wound to her right shoulder, and the effort of using the mind trick on the Inquisitors nearly killed her.[[79]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_7-79)

##### Hunt for Eeth Koth[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Hunt for Eeth Koth](/wiki/Hunt_for_Eeth_Koth "Hunt for Eeth Koth")

:   "*To one less Jedi in the galaxy.*"
:   ―[Tualon Yaluna](/wiki/Tualon_Yaluna "Tualon Yaluna"), toasting to the death of Eeth Koth[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2)

Eventually, Darth Vader and the Inquisitorius [located](/wiki/Hunt_for_Eeth_Koth "Hunt for Eeth Koth") the former Jedi Master [Eeth Koth](/wiki/Eeth_Koth "Eeth Koth"), who had left the Order during the Clone Wars. Vader found Koth with his [wife](/wiki/Mira_(Zabrak) "Mira (Zabrak)"), who had just given birth. Sending[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2) [Thirteenth Sister](/wiki/Thirteenth_Sister "Thirteenth Sister")[[20]](#cite_note-Inquisitor:_Rise_of_the_Red_Blade-20) to secure the [child](/wiki/Eeth_Koth%27s_daughter "Eeth Koth's daughter"), Vader engaged Koth in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel"). Once the child was secured, Vader stabbed Koth in the back, killing him.[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2)

##### Mission to rebuild the Jedi Order[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Secret mission to rebuild the Jedi Order](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_rebuild_the_Jedi_Order "Secret mission to rebuild the Jedi Order")

:   "*We seek a dangerous fugitive. This is no common anarchist but a devotee of the treasonous Jedi Order. Failure to turn over this traitor will result in a charge of sedition. Turn yourself in or everyone present shall face summary execution.*"
:   ―The Second Sister, to a group of workers on Bracca[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1)

 [![The surviving Jedi Cal Kestis rose up against the Empire and tried to rebuild the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/Cal_Kestis_force_push_JFO.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191124142210) [![The surviving Jedi Cal Kestis rose up against the Empire and tried to rebuild the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/Cal_Kestis_force_push_JFO.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20191124142210)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a2/Cal_Kestis_force_push_JFO.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20191124142210) 

The surviving Jedi Cal Kestis rose up against the Empire and tried to rebuild the Jedi Order.

 

In [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY"),[[80]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order_date-80) the Inquisitorius discovered a Jedi, the Padawan [Cal Kestis](/wiki/Cal_Kestis "Cal Kestis"), hidden on [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca"). The [Second Sister](/wiki/Second_Sister "Second Sister") and Ninth Sister were sent to kill him, but Kestis managed to escape. The Ninth Sister was [defeated](/wiki/Liberation_on_Kashyyyk "Liberation on Kashyyyk") by Kestis on Kashyyyk, and the Second Sister met her death in [Nur](/wiki/Nur "Nur") after being [defeated](/wiki/Mission_to_Nur "Mission to Nur") by Kestis and moving away from the dark side of the Force, having reconciled with her former Jedi master, [Cere Junda](/wiki/Cere_Junda "Cere Junda"), whom Kestis joined and consecrated him a [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"). Darth Vader arrived in time to see the Second Sister's betrayal and execute her with his lightsaber. Vader tried to kill Kestis and Junda, but both narrowly escaped.[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1)

 [![Kestis' fight against the Empire began when the Second Sister began a hunt for him.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/CalVsTrilla.png/revision/latest?cb=20210519104858) [![Kestis' fight against the Empire began when the Second Sister began a hunt for him.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/CalVsTrilla.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210519104858)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ef/CalVsTrilla.png/revision/latest?cb=20210519104858) 

Kestis' fight against the Empire began when the Second Sister began a hunt for him.

 

Having seen a [Force vision](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision") that predicted his potential Jedi academy would be found and destroyed, Kestis decided to destroy [Eno Cordova's holocron](/wiki/Eno_Cordova%27s_holocron "Eno Cordova's holocron"), which contained a list of Force-sensitive children across the galaxy that Kestis and Junda intended to use to rebuild the Jedi Order, which had been retrieved on Nur. Kestis felt that the children's fate should be entrusted to [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"). Afterward, he asked what they should do next.[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1)

##### Hunt for Tensu Run[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Conquest of Regis Kor](/wiki/Conquest_of_Regis_Kor "Conquest of Regis Kor") and [Hunt for Tensu Run](/wiki/Hunt_for_Tensu_Run "Hunt for Tensu Run")

:   "*I commanded you to bring the head of Tensu Run at my feet.*"
:   ―Darth Vader, to the Grand Inquisitor[[24]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_1-24)

 [![After an intense hunt, Tensu Run, one of the Inquisitorius' most important targets, met his end by the hands of Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/TensuRunDeath-Inquisitors4.png/revision/latest?cb=20241217004833) [![After an intense hunt, Tensu Run, one of the Inquisitorius' most important targets, met his end by the hands of Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/TensuRunDeath-Inquisitors4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20241217004833)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/56/TensuRunDeath-Inquisitors4.png/revision/latest?cb=20241217004833) 

After an intense hunt, Tensu Run, one of the Inquisitorius' most important targets, met his end by the hands of Darth Vader.

 

Jedi Knight [Tensu Run](/wiki/Tensu_Run "Tensu Run") became a threat to the Empire, as after freeing prisoners from an [Imperial outpost](/wiki/Imperial_outpost_(Regis_Kor) "Imperial outpost (Regis Kor)") during the [Conquest of Regis Kor](/wiki/Conquest_of_Regis_Kor "Conquest of Regis Kor"), he became a symbol of hope. Tensu Run's [death](/wiki/Death "Death") became one of the Inquisitorius' highest priorities, with [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"),[[24]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_1-24) the [Fifth Brother](/wiki/Fifth_Brother "Fifth Brother"),[[81]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_2-81) the [Seventh Sister](/wiki/Seventh_Sister "Seventh Sister"), and the [Ninth Sister](/wiki/Ninth_Sister "Ninth Sister"),[[82]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_3-82) all participating in the [hunt](/wiki/Hunt_for_Tensu_Run "Hunt for Tensu Run"). The Inquisitors were defeated more than once by the Jedi Knight, who, along with other survivors of Order 66, sought to restore the Jedi Order. Due to the Inquisitors' failures, Darth Vader led the four Inquisitors in a final confrontation with the Jedi, which resulted in Run's death by the hands of the Sith Lord, as well as the other Jedi, who were eliminated by the Inquisitors.[[16]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_4-16)

##### Hunt for Kenobi and the Hidden Path[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main articles: [Hunt for Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Hunt_for_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Hunt for Obi-Wan Kenobi") and [Hunt for the Hidden Path](/wiki/Hunt_for_the_Hidden_Path "Hunt for the Hidden Path")

 [![Reva Sevander joined the Inquisitorius to get closer to Darth Vader and wait for the right moment to take revenge on the Sith Lord.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/ThirdSisterThreat-KenobiPartI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220704152153) [![Reva Sevander joined the Inquisitorius to get closer to Darth Vader and wait for the right moment to take revenge on the Sith Lord.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/ThirdSisterThreat-KenobiPartI.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220704152153)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/98/ThirdSisterThreat-KenobiPartI.png/revision/latest?cb=20220704152153) 

Reva Sevander joined the Inquisitorius to get closer to Darth Vader and wait for the right moment to take revenge on the Sith Lord.

 

One Inquisitor, the "Third Sister" [Reva Sevander](/wiki/Reva_Sevander "Reva Sevander"), was secretly working to kill Vader[[25]](#cite_note-Kenobi_V-25) so as to avenge her fellow Jedi younglings he killed during Order 66.[[83]](#cite_note-Kenobi_VI-83) Unknown to her, Vader was aware of her plan. So as to get close to Vader, Sevander worked to continue the [hunt for Obi-Wan](/wiki/Hunt_for_Obi-Wan "Hunt for Obi-Wan") Kenobi despite a lack of leads on the case.[[25]](#cite_note-Kenobi_V-25) Meanwhile, the Inquisitorius was also carrying out a [hunt](/wiki/Hunt_for_the_Hidden_Path "Hunt for the Hidden Path") for the [Hidden Path](/wiki/Hidden_Path "Hidden Path") network,[[26]](#cite_note-Kenobi_IV-26) which worked to smuggle Force-sensitives to safety away from the Empire's eyes.[[32]](#cite_note-Kenobi_III-32) One of its members was the [con artist](/wiki/Con_artist "Con artist") [Haja Estree](/wiki/Haja_Estree "Haja Estree"), who pretended to be a Jedi on the crime ridden planet [Daiyu](/wiki/Daiyu "Daiyu"): while Estree did indeed scam people for credits, he did ensure those who came to him for help got it.[[84]](#cite_note-Part_II-84)

Uncovering a link between Senator Bail Organa and Kenobi, Sevander dispatched a team of criminals led by [Vect Nokru](/wiki/Vect_Nokru "Vect Nokru") to [ambush and kidnap](/wiki/Ambush_on_Alderaan "Ambush on Alderaan") Organa's adoptive daughter Leia. Meanwhile, Sevander was part of a [hunt](/wiki/Search_for_Nari "Search for Nari") for the surviving Jedi [Nari](/wiki/Nari "Nari") that took herself, the Grand Inquisitor, and the Fifth Brother to Tatooine, where Nari found an emotionally broken Kenobi who refused to help him. Ultimately, Nari would be killed. At the urging of Organa, Kenobi, traveled offworld[[27]](#cite_note-Kenobi_I-27) and rescued Leia on Daiyu. Uncovering the Third Sister's plot, the Grand Inquisitor, Fifth Brother, and [Fourth Sister](/wiki/Fourth_Sister "Fourth Sister") also traveled to Daiyu with their stormtrooper forces to reprimand Sevander and capture Kenobi without her. With Estree's help, Kenobi and Organa managed to escape the planet, but not before a run-in with the Third Sister: she stabbed the Grand Inquisitor to get him out of her way and revealed to Kenobi that Vader was alive.[[84]](#cite_note-Part_II-84)

Journeying to the mining planet [Mapuzo](/wiki/Mapuzo "Mapuzo") in the Mid Rim, Kenobi and Organa reached a [Path safehouse](/wiki/Mapuzo_safehouse "Mapuzo safehouse") operated by undercover Imperial captain [Tala Durith](/wiki/Tala_Durith "Tala Durith") and the droid [NED-B](/wiki/NED-B "NED-B"). However, Vader himself arrived with the Inquisitors and handily bested Kenobi[[32]](#cite_note-Kenobi_III-32) in the [battle on Mapuzo](/wiki/Battle_on_Mapuzo "Battle on Mapuzo").[[85]](#cite_note-Decoding_Darth-85) While Durith managed to get Kenobi out alive and bring him to the Path base of operations on the planet [Jabiim](/wiki/Jabiim "Jabiim"),[[26]](#cite_note-Kenobi_IV-26) Organa was captured by the Third Sister[[32]](#cite_note-Kenobi_III-32) and brought to the Fortress Inquisitorius for questioning. Kenobi and Durith [infiltrated the base](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia_(9_BBY) "Rescue of Princess Leia (9 BBY)"), rescued Organa, and escaped. Pointed to Jabiim by a tracking device hidden within Organa's droid [L0-LA59](/wiki/L0-LA59 "L0-LA59"),[[26]](#cite_note-Kenobi_IV-26) Sevander, promoted to the rank of Grand Inquisitor by Vader, led an [Imperial assault on the Path base](/wiki/Attack_on_Jabiim "Attack on Jabiim"), where Durith gave her life to hold back the Empire.[[25]](#cite_note-Kenobi_V-25)

 [![The second rematch between Obi-Wan Kenobi and Darth Vader on a barren moon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/TheConfrontation-KarlFitzgerald.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126211951) [![The second rematch between Obi-Wan Kenobi and Darth Vader on a barren moon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/TheConfrontation-KarlFitzgerald.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20231126211951)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9f/TheConfrontation-KarlFitzgerald.png/revision/latest?cb=20231126211951) 

The second rematch between Obi-Wan Kenobi and Darth Vader on a barren moon.

 

Kenobi, who put together that Sevander was working against Vader, deduced how his former disciple would think by distracting him with an empty transport. Kenobi, Organa, and the rest of the Path soon escaped aboard Roken's freight transport, while Sevander made her move against Vader, who handily defeated her before revealing the Grand Inquisitor's survival. Both left[[25]](#cite_note-Kenobi_V-25) to pursue the fleeing transport aboard the *[Devastator](/wiki/Devastator "Devastator")*, while Sevander made her way to Tatooine[[83]](#cite_note-Kenobi_VI-83) after discovering the existence of Luke Skywalker from a holoprojector Kenobi dropped in the chaos.[[25]](#cite_note-Kenobi_V-25) Knowing Vader was more interested in him than the Path as a whole, Kenobi drew the *Devastator* off the transport's trail by heading to a [barren moon](/wiki/Unidentified_barren_moon "Unidentified barren moon"), where Kenobi found faith in the future through his experiences with Luke and Leia. Kenobi defeated Vader in the [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Fight_on_a_barren_moon "Fight on a barren moon") and left Vader beaten. Kenobi then returned to Tatooine, where he had felt Skywalker was in danger; Sevander [attacked](/wiki/Assault_on_the_Lars_Homestead "Assault on the Lars Homestead") the [Lars Homestead](/wiki/Lars_homestead "Lars homestead") in an effort to kill the boy but ultimately was unable to go through with the act. Assured by Kenobi that re-embracing the light was better for the memory of her lost friends, Sevander rejected her station as an Inquisitor.[[83]](#cite_note-Kenobi_VI-83)

After his failure to capture Kenobi, Vader dispatched [probe droids](/wiki/Probe_droid "Probe droid") to find the Jedi Master and reported his progress to Sidious, who ordered Vader to stop so as to not let his past define him. Organa was returned home to Alderaan and bid goodbye to Kenobi, who also promised to help battle the growing power of the Empire if he was needed, when he visited. With his hope restored, Kenobi also finally saw the Force spirit of his former master, Qui-Gon Jinn.[[83]](#cite_note-Kenobi_VI-83)

##### A refuge for those persecuted by the Empire[]

:   "*Tanalorr's a fortress. We should use it for the Hidden Path. Gather allies. Train. They'd never see us coming.*"
:   ―Cal Kestis[[3]](#cite_note-Survivor-3)

 [![Kestis intended to make Tanalorr a haven for those persecuted by the Empire, including Force-users.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/Tanalorr_SWJediSurvivor.png/revision/latest?cb=20230429060921) [![Kestis intended to make Tanalorr a haven for those persecuted by the Empire, including Force-users.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/Tanalorr_SWJediSurvivor.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/184?cb=20230429060921)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/36/Tanalorr_SWJediSurvivor.png/revision/latest?cb=20230429060921) 

Kestis intended to make Tanalorr a haven for those persecuted by the Empire, including Force-users.

 

Over the five years following the holocron's destruction, Kestis has become an extremely important target for the Empire, having attracted the attention of not only the Inquisitorius, but the [ISB](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") as well.[[3]](#cite_note-Survivor-3) In [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"),[[86]](#cite_note-Survivor_date-86) on the planet [Koboh](/wiki/Koboh "Koboh"), Kestis encountered something from the Jedi's golden age. Kestis encountered the Jedi [Dagan Gera](/wiki/Dagan_Gera "Dagan Gera"), who has been preserved in bacta since the days of the High Republic. Kestis freed the old Jedi and asked for his help in his fight against the Empire. However, Gera fell out with the Jedi Order, who he believed had betrayed him because the Jedi had given up on [Tanalorr](/wiki/Tanalorr "Tanalorr"), a hard-to-reach world Dagan had become obsessed with, after an [attack](/wiki/Attack_on_Tanalorr "Attack on Tanalorr") by the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil"). Gera fell to the dark side and bled the kyber crystal from his lightsaber, starting a duel with Kestis afterwards. Dagan escaped with the help of his old ally, the [Gen'Dai](/wiki/Gen%27Dai "Gen'Dai") [Rayvis](/wiki/Rayvis "Rayvis"), and intended to return to Tanalorr and create an army led by Force-users trained by himself to fight the Empire. However, due to the clouded view of Gera by the dark side, Kestis opposed his plan. Along with [Bode Akuna](/wiki/Bode_Akuna "Bode Akuna"), Kestis killed Dagan and obtained the compass that would guide them to Tanalorr, a place that Kestis intended to transform into a refuge for those persecuted by the Empire.[[3]](#cite_note-Survivor-3)

 [![After the funeral, Kestis promised to honor Cere's legacy by building something that would outlast the Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/Funeral_on_Tanalorr.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230501052547) [![After the funeral, Kestis promised to honor Cere's legacy by building something that would outlast the Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/Funeral_on_Tanalorr.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/206?cb=20230501052547)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/Funeral_on_Tanalorr.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230501052547) 

After the funeral, Kestis promised to honor Cere's legacy by building something that would outlast the Empire.

 

However, the compass was stolen by Akuna, who was an ISB's spy and a survivor of the Jedi Purge. Akuna intended to flee to Tanalorr with he daughter so that they could live free from the Empire forever, which, in he opinion, Kestis' intentions for Tanalorr jeopardized. Kestis followed Akuna to Tanalorr, and along with his ally, the [Nightsister](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") [Merrin](/wiki/Merrin "Merrin"), slew him. Kestis and his friends took in Bode's daughter and held a Jedi funeral for Akuna, Cere Junda, and [Eno Cordova](/wiki/Eno_Cordova "Eno Cordova"), who were trying to restore knowledge from the Jedi archives and were killed due to Akuna stealing the compass. With the compass to cross the deadly [Koboh Abyss](/wiki/Koboh_Abyss "Koboh Abyss") [nebula](/wiki/Nebula "Nebula"), Kestis and his allies began to prepare Tanalorr for use by the [Hidden Path](/wiki/Hidden_Path "Hidden Path").[[3]](#cite_note-Survivor-3)

##### Uprising on Lothal[]

:   "*The Emperor has foreseen a new threat rising against him: the children of the Force. They must not become Jedi.*"  
    "*Yes, Lord Vader.*"  
    "*Hunt down this new enemy, and if they will not serve the Empire, eliminate them along with any surviving Jedi who would train them. This is my master's command.*"
:   ―Darth Vader and the Grand Inquisitor[[87]](#cite_note-Spark_of_Rebellion-87)

As the Empire expanded throughout the galaxy, and the Sith increased their hold over the cosmos, the Emperor sensed a new threat that could potentially rise against him. This threat, which Darth Vader referred to as the "children of the Force," came in the form of young Force-sensitives who the Emperor feared would rise up against the Empire. The Inquisitors were ordered to either turn these individuals to the dark side or eliminate them, along with any Jedi who could potentially train them. To that end, the Inquisitors carried out an operation known as [Project Harvester](/wiki/Project_Harvester "Project Harvester") to capture these young Force-sensitive beings.[[88]](#cite_note-Rebel_in_the_Ranks-88) These individuals were recruited from such facilities as the [Imperial Academy](/wiki/Academy_for_Young_Imperials "Academy for Young Imperials") on the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") world of [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal") or were taken from their parents as infants.[[89]](#cite_note-Breaking_Ranks-89)

 [![Knight Kanan Jarrus and Padawan Ezra Bridger emerged as enemies of the Empire and, eventually, the Sith during the Imperial Era.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Rebels_protect_Trayvis.png/revision/latest?cb=20150127160710) [![Knight Kanan Jarrus and Padawan Ezra Bridger emerged as enemies of the Empire and, eventually, the Sith during the Imperial Era.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Rebels_protect_Trayvis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20150127160710)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Rebels_protect_Trayvis.png/revision/latest?cb=20150127160710) 

Knight Kanan Jarrus and Padawan Ezra Bridger emerged as enemies of the Empire and, eventually, the Sith during the Imperial Era.

 

The Age of the Empire also led to a number of rebel cells operating throughout the galaxy in opposition of the Empire. One such cell was the [Spectres](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres") rebel cell that based on Lothal, and was was led by [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla") of the [starship](/wiki/Starship "Starship") *[Ghost](/wiki/Ghost "Ghost")*, as well as Caleb Dume,[[87]](#cite_note-Spark_of_Rebellion-87) who took on the name Kanan Jarrus in order to evade Imperial execution.[[90]](#cite_note-A_New_Dawn-90) The cell came to the attention of the Empire after Jarrus revealed himself as a Jedi while [freeing](/wiki/Mission_to_free_Wookiee_prisoners "Mission to free Wookiee prisoners") [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") [slaves](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") from the [spice mines](/wiki/Spice_mines_of_Kessel "Spice mines of Kessel") of the planet [Kessel](/wiki/Kessel "Kessel").[[87]](#cite_note-Spark_of_Rebellion-87) The Empire tracked down Jarrus and [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"), who had become Jarrus's Padawan apprentice, and they too were lured into the Spire, but they managed to escape before they were killed.[[7]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Old_Masters-7)

Later, the Spectres sabotaged the [Empire Day](/wiki/Empire_Day "Empire Day") celebrations at Lothal's [Capital City](/wiki/Capital_City "Capital City")[[91]](#cite_note-Empire_Day-91) in [4 BBY](/wiki/4_BBY "4 BBY")[[92]](#cite_note-Empire_Day_date-92) and rescued the [Rodian](/wiki/Rodian "Rodian") [Imperial Information Office](/wiki/Imperial_Information_Office "Imperial Information Office") employee [Tseebo](/wiki/Tseebo "Tseebo"). The Grand Inquisitor pursued the Spectres, but they escaped into hyperspace aboard the *Ghost*.[[91]](#cite_note-Empire_Day-91) However, the Grand Inquisitor tracked down the Spectres using an [XX-23 S-thread tracker](/wiki/XX-23_S-thread_tracker "XX-23 S-thread tracker") attacked to the auxiliary shuttle *[Phantom](/wiki/Phantom "Phantom")*. While the other crew members spirited Tseebo away into hiding, Bridger and Jarrus led the Grand Inquisitor to [Fort Anaxes](/wiki/Fort_Anaxes "Fort Anaxes") on [PM-1203](/wiki/PM-1203 "PM-1203"). Following a brief duel, the two Jedi escaped the Inquisitor. However, Bridger tapped into the dark side in a moment of fear.[[93]](#cite_note-Gathering_Forces-93)

Due to the failure of the Inquisitor and other Imperial agents to capture the Spectres and their Jedi "leader," [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") arrived on Lothal and chastised them for their failings. Working with the [Imperial Security Bureau](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") [Agent](/wiki/Agent "Agent") [Kallus](/wiki/Alexsandr_Kallus "Alexsandr Kallus") and Tarkin, the Grand Inquisitor [trapped](/wiki/Raid_on_the_communications_tower "Raid on the communications tower") the Spectres at the [Imperial Communications Center](/wiki/Imperial_Communications_Center "Imperial Communications Center") near Jalath. The Inquisitor bested Jarrus in combat and captured the Jedi.
