However, the other Spectres escaped and used a [computer spike](/wiki/Computer_spike "Computer spike") to hijack the communications tower and broadcast Bridger's message of rebellion.[[94]](#cite_note-Call_to_Action-94) After the Grand Inquisitor and Kallus proved unable to break Jarrus, Tarkin advocated transferring the Jedi to Mustafar, a place "where the Jedi went to die."[[95]](#cite_note-Rebel_Resolve-95)

Above Mustafar, the Grand Inquisitor continued interrogating Jarrus aboard Tarkin's [Imperial Star Destroyer](/wiki/Imperial-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial-class Star Destroyer") *[Sovereign](/wiki/Sovereign "Sovereign")*; taunting Jarrus about the death of his master Billaba. However, Jarrus' comrades infiltrated the *Sovereign*, and Bridger rescued his master. Jarrus then defeated the Grand Inquisitor in a [duel](/wiki/Action_at_Mustafar "Action at Mustafar") aboard the Star Destroyer's reactor core. Rather than face the penalty for his failure, the Grand Inquisitor committed [suicide](/wiki/Death "Death") by plunging into the malfunctioning reactor. The Spectres escaped Tarkin's stricken Star Destroyer with the help of [Phoenix Cell](/wiki/Phoenix_Cell "Phoenix Cell"), a larger rebel cell. They were also greeted by Tano, who revealed herself as the rebel spymaster [Fulcrum](/wiki/Fulcrum "Fulcrum").[[8]](#cite_note-FATG-8)

### Galactic Civil War[]

##### Hunt for the rebel Jedi[]

Shortly afterward, the Emperor sent Darth Vader to deal with the rebel threat, as the rebels began working with the larger rebel movement led by Senator Organa and Tano,[[8]](#cite_note-FATG-8) the former Padawan of Anakin Skywalker. Following a botched mission to rescue [Minister](/wiki/Minister "Minister") [Maketh Tua](/wiki/Maketh_Tua "Maketh Tua"), Vader ambushed the Spectres at the [Imperial Complex](/wiki/Imperial_Complex_(Lothal) "Imperial Complex (Lothal)") on Lothal. Despite besting Jarrus and Bridger in [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat"), the Spectres managed to escape back to the Phoenix fleet. However, Vader [pursued](/wiki/Attack_on_Phoenix_Squadron_(4_BBY) "Attack on Phoenix Squadron (4 BBY)") them in his [TIE Advanced x1](/wiki/TIE_Advanced_x1 "TIE Advanced x1") and crippled the rebel flagship *[Phoenix Home](/wiki/Phoenix_Home "Phoenix Home")*. During the dogfight, Tano and Vader sensed each other's presence in the Force. This encounter confirmed her survival to Vader, while Tano later denied knowing who Vader was. After the Phoenix Squadron escaped with the Jedi fugitives, the Emperor ordered his apprentice to send another Inquisitor to deal with the situation.[[28]](#cite_note-The_Siege_of_Lothal-28) At some point, an [Inquisitor](/wiki/Unidentified_Inquisitor_(Karalle) "Unidentified Inquisitor (Karalle)") hunted the Force-sensitive [Jarea Kaela](/wiki/Jarea_Kaela "Jarea Kaela") and spread the rumor that the Force-sensitive [Quermian](/wiki/Quermian "Quermian") was a witch.[[96]](#cite_note-Savage-96)

During the [Assault](/wiki/Assault_on_Seelos "Assault on Seelos") on [Seelos](/wiki/Seelos "Seelos"), [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Kassius Konstantine](/wiki/Kassius_Konstantine "Kassius Konstantine") was ordered to rendezvous with the [Fifth Brother](/wiki/Fifth_Brother "Fifth Brother") in space. While Konstantine was concerned that this rendezvous had compromised the Imperial Security Bureau Agent Kallus' mission on Seelos, the Fifth Brother was unperturbed and vowed to succeed where Konstantine and Kallus had failed.[[97]](#cite_note-ROTOR-97) Later, the [Seventh Sister](/wiki/Seventh_Sister "Seventh Sister") and the Fifth Brother ambushed members of the Spectres rebel cell at an abandoned Republic [*Haven*-class medical station](/wiki/Haven-class_medical_station "Haven-class medical station") in space. One of the Spectres was Bridger, who clashed with both the Seventh Sister and the Fifth Brother in lightsaber combat. Following a [brief skirmish](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_a_Republic_medical_station "Skirmish aboard a Republic medical station"), the Spectres escaped back to Phoenix Group on the *Phantom*. Bridger related his encounter to Jarrus, who was shocked that there was more than one Inquisitor.[[98]](#cite_note-ATTA-98)

##### The Seventh and the Fifth[]

The Seventh Sister and the Fifth Brother then embarked on a campaign to abduct Force-sensitive children for the Empire and kidnapped baby [Alora](/wiki/Alora "Alora") from her grandmother [Darja](/wiki/Darja "Darja"). Tano learned about the Inquisitors' secondary mission and enlisted Jarrus and Bridger's help in stopping them. Tracking the Inquisitor's coordinates, Jarrus, Bridger, [Garazeb Orrelios](/wiki/Garazeb_Orrelios "Garazeb Orrelios"), and [Chopper](/wiki/C1-10P "C1-10P") traveled to the planet [Takobo](/wiki/Takobo "Takobo"). They managed to rescue the [Ithorian](/wiki/Ithorian "Ithorian") baby [Pypey](/wiki/Pypey "Pypey") from the Inquisitors but were unable to match them in combat. Tano came to their rescue and the Jedi and rebels escaped aboard the *Phantom*. With the Jedi Order gone, Tano, Jarrus, and Bridger resolved to protect Force-sensitive children from the Empire.[[99]](#cite_note-The_Future_of_the_Force-99)

Acting on information obtained by one of the Seventh Sister's [ID9 seeker droids](/wiki/ID9_seeker_droid "ID9 seeker droid"), the Seventh Sister and Fifth Brother later joined forces with Agent Kallus and Admiral Konstantine to [hunt down and destroy](/wiki/Battle_of_Garel "Battle of Garel") the Phoenix Squadron, which was hiding on the planet [Garel](/wiki/Garel "Garel"). The two Inquisitors caught up with Bridger and Jarrus but the Spectres escaped aboard the *Ghost* into space.[[100]](#cite_note-Legacy-100)

For the next several months, the Seventh Sister and the Fifth Brother continued their hunt for Bridger and Jarrus, [undermining](/wiki/Duel_on_Oosalon "Duel on Oosalon") their efforts to help Phoenix Squadron find a new base on [Oosalon](/wiki/Oosalon "Oosalon"). In desperation, Bridger, Jarrus, and Tano visited the [Lothal Jedi Temple](/wiki/Lothal_Jedi_Temple "Lothal Jedi Temple") to seek out wisdom in this hour of crisis. There, Bridger communed with Yoda, who told the young Padawan to find [Malachor](/wiki/Malachor "Malachor"). Meanwhile, Jarrus completed his [Jedi Trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials") and emerged a Jedi Knight while Tano confronted her suspicion that Skywalker and Vader were one and the same. The trio escaped the Lothal Jedi Temple before the Fifth Brother and Seventh Sister forced their way into the temple. The two Inquisitors then informed Vader about their finding.[[101]](#cite_note-Shroud-101)

##### End of the purge[]

:   "*There are no Jedi! You and your Inquisitors have seen to that. […] I am no Jedi.*"
:   ―Ahsoka Tano, to Darth Vader[[29]](#cite_note-Twilight-29)

After helping Phoenix Squadron to establish [Chopper Base](/wiki/Chopper_Base "Chopper Base") on the planet [Atollon](/wiki/Atollon "Atollon"), Jarrus and Bridger accompanied Tano to the planet Malachor, intent on [finding](/wiki/Mission_to_Malachor "Mission to Malachor") the secrets to destroying the Sith. There, they were attacked by the [Eighth Brother](/wiki/Eighth_Brother "Eighth Brother"). Ezra was separated from Jarrus and Tano and encountered the former Sith apprentice Maul, who offered to help him obtain the secrets inside the [Malachor Sith Temple](/wiki/Malachor_Sith_Temple "Malachor Sith Temple"). After Maul helped the Jedi and Tano to fight off the Eighth Brother, Seventh Sister, and Fifth Brother, they reluctantly teamed up with Maul to obtain the temple's secrets. While Bridger was convinced that Maul was an ally, Jarrus and Tano distrusted the former Sith.[[29]](#cite_note-Twilight-29)

 [![Though Ahsoka Tano no longer considered herself a Jedi, she was nonetheless marked for death under Order 66.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Master_versus_the_apprentice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160403150039) [![Though Ahsoka Tano no longer considered herself a Jedi, she was nonetheless marked for death under Order 66.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Master_versus_the_apprentice.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160403150039)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/Master_versus_the_apprentice.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160403150039) 

Though Ahsoka Tano no longer considered herself a Jedi, she was nonetheless marked for death under Order 66.

 

Maul convinced Bridger to place the [Sith holocron](/wiki/Sith_holocron_(Malachor) "Sith holocron (Malachor)") they had recovered inside the Sith temple's obelisk. After killing the Inquisitors, Maul then turned on Jarrus and Tano, blinding the former. Meanwhile, Bridger learned that the Sith temple was an ancient battle station capable of destroying all life and refused to harness the Temple's dark-side powers. However, Vader arrived and fought Bridger, only to be confronted by Tano; denying his request to join him and hunt any surviving Jedi, going so far as to say Vader and his Inquisitors had destroyed the last of the Order, Tano affirmed she was not a Jedi and battled Vader in the name of avenging Anakin Skywalker. Bridger and his blinded master managed to escape with Chopper aboard the *Phantom* while Tano stayed behind to hold back Vader. After the Sith temple imploded, Vader departed while Tano headed inside the temple.[[29]](#cite_note-Twilight-29) With Tano assumed dead, the Great Jedi Purge came to its end.[[11]](#cite_note-Odyssey-11)

## Aftermath[]

### Fall of Maul[]

:   "*Tell me… Is it the Chosen One?*"  
    "*He is.*"  
    "*He… will… avenge us.*"
:   ―Maul's final words with Obi-Wan Kenobi, referencing Luke Skywalker[[102]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-102)

Later, Maul [captured](/wiki/Maul%27s_capture_of_the_Ghost_crew "Maul's capture of the Ghost crew") the Spectres to force Bridger and Jarrus to bring the [Sith holocron](/wiki/Sith_holocron "Sith holocron") from Malachor and the [latter's Jedi holocron](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus%27_holocron "Kanan Jarrus' holocron") to him. After learning an individual with a red lightsaber was behind the capture, Bridger initially speculated that another Inquisitor was responsible, though they soon learned it was Maul.[[103]](#cite_note-THOF-103)

Maul later manipulated Bridger into helping him find Obi-Wan Kenobi on Tatooine. After Kenobi sent Bridger away and Maul deduced that Kenobi was protecting someone on the planet, the Jedi Master and his old enemy engaged in [one final duel](/wiki/Mission_to_Tatooine_(Imperial_Era) "Mission to Tatooine (Imperial Era)"), which Kenobi quickly ended by fatally striking the former Sith. As Maul died in his nemesis's arms, he asked if the person Kenobi was guarding, secretly Anakin Skywalker's son Luke, was the Chosen One. Kenobi believed this was the case, and Maul died hoping the young Skywalker would avenge them.[[102]](#cite_note-Twin_Suns-102)

### Lothal's final stand[]

:   [![icon](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/04/Blue_Glass_Arrow.svg/revision/latest?cb=20090726033133) Main article: [Lothal campaign](/wiki/Lothal_campaign "Lothal campaign")

:   "*Hmm, the Jedi once numbered in the thousands. What's left are a scattered, frightened lot, mostly beaten and in hiding, or poorly trained children, like yourself.*"
:   ―Grand Admiral Thrawn, to Ezra Bridger[[104]](#cite_note-Family&Farewell-104)

During the [mission to Batuu](/wiki/Mission_to_Batuu_(Galactic_Empire) "Mission to Batuu (Galactic Empire)"), Darth Vader reflected on how the war against the Jedi Order had been won.[[105]](#cite_note-Thrawn_Alliances-105) Still, even as the Empire and the consolidated Rebel forces that had come to be known as the [Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") fought, several Jedi had survived the purge. Among these survivors were Jarrus and Bridger, but, after the Spectres' return to Lothal, the former gave his life [to protect](/wiki/Rescue_of_Hera_Syndulla_(Lothal) "Rescue of Hera Syndulla (Lothal)") Bridger, fellow rebel [Sabine Wren](/wiki/Sabine_Wren "Sabine Wren"), and his lover, the now-General Syndulla.[[106]](#cite_note-Jedi_Night-106)

 [![Kanan Jarrus sacrificed himself to protect his family.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/KananJarrusFinalMoments-JediNight.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240309195507) [![Kanan Jarrus sacrificed himself to protect his family.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/KananJarrusFinalMoments-JediNight.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240309195507)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e9/KananJarrusFinalMoments-JediNight.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240309195507) 

Kanan Jarrus sacrificed himself to protect his family.

 

Shortly afterward, the Spectres launched a [mission to the Lothal Jedi Temple](/wiki/Mission_to_the_Lothal_Jedi_Temple "Mission to the Lothal Jedi Temple"), leading to Bridger entering the [World Between Worlds](/wiki/World_Between_Worlds "World Between Worlds") through a portal, which enabled him to reach through time and save Tano from Vader on Malachor. The two were interrupted by Darth Sidious, who tried to use Bridger to access the World Between Worlds, which would have given the Galactic Emperor control of the universe itself. The two escaped Palpatine, and Tano returned to her own point in time, though she promised Bridger she would find him again, while Bridger returned to his friends outside the portal. The Lothal Jedi Temple collapsed, thus destroying the gateway into the World Between Worlds.[[107]](#cite_note-Worlds-107)

A short time later, Bridger, the other Spectres, and their assorted allies launched an [attempt](/wiki/Liberation_of_Lothal "Liberation of Lothal") to liberate Lothal, during which the Jedi Padawan was captured and taken to [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo") on the *[Chimaera](/wiki/Chimaera "Chimaera")*. During their conversation, Bridger and Thrawn discussed the Jedi, with the [Imperial officer](/wiki/Imperial_officer "Imperial officer") noting that the majority of the Order's members were either in hiding or "poorly trained children." Thrawn took the Force-sensitive before Sidious, who spoke to Bridger via a hologram. Through a surviving part of the Lothal temple he had ordered be brought aboard the Star Destroyer, the Sith Lord offered the young man a chance to reunite with his parents. The Jedi Padawan ultimately refused the potential future and destroyed the temple fragment, again denying Sidious access to the World Between Worlds.[[104]](#cite_note-Family&Farewell-104)

 [![Ezra Bridger made a final stand to liberate his home planet.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Ezras_Wolf_Pack_AFH.png/revision/latest?cb=20180904235758) [![Ezra Bridger made a final stand to liberate his home planet.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Ezras_Wolf_Pack_AFH.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180904235758)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Ezras_Wolf_Pack_AFH.png/revision/latest?cb=20180904235758) 

Ezra Bridger made a final stand to liberate his home planet.

 

Escaping three [Royal Guards](/wiki/Emperor%27s_Royal_Guard "Emperor's Royal Guard") and a trio of [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper"), Bridger made his way to the *Chimaera*'s [bridge](/wiki/Bridge_(starship) "Bridge (starship)"), where he confronted Thrawn. Thanks to a pod of [Purrgil](/wiki/Purrgil "Purrgil") he had asked the young rebel [Mart Mattin](/wiki/Mart_Mattin "Mart Mattin") to summon, the [Seventh Fleet](/wiki/Seventh_Fleet_(Galactic_Empire) "Seventh Fleet (Galactic Empire)") was defeated, and the *Chimaera*, including Bridger, Thrawn, and all others aboard, was taken away into hyperspace by the creatures. With the Imperial fleet gone, the Spectres and their allies, having lured all Imperial forces into the structure with a false [Protocol 13](/wiki/Protocol_13 "Protocol 13"), destroyed the Empire's command "dome," fulfilling Bridger's wish that his homeworld be freed from Imperial oppression.[[104]](#cite_note-Family&Farewell-104)

### Continued actions[]

:   "*At the end of the Clone Wars, when Emperor Palpatine took power, he declared the entire Jedi Order to be traitors. He issued Order 66, and most of the Jedi died that very day. Not just full Knights either. Padawans, younglings. That was the purge. Order 66 still stands. Jedi are to be killed on sight. Even people who might be Jedi. People like me. That's why I ran when you first saw me. The Empire sent out powerful Force-users, dark side adepts, to hunt down any Jedi survivors. They were called the Inquisitorius. But their boss... he was worse than any of them. And he's still out there. The monster of monsters. Pure, true evil. Darth Vader.*"
:   ―Verla, to Luke Skywalker[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_5-65)

Despite the formal ending of the Great Jedi Purge,[[11]](#cite_note-Odyssey-11) Order 66 remained in effect, resulting the continued execution of any surviving Jedi or could-be Jedi on sight. Verla, for example, had spent years running from the Inquisitors and Vader[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_5-65) and developed a jaded view of the Force,[[108]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_6-108) further thinking it was foolish to continue her Jedi training.[[65]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_5-65)

Nonetheless, with the apparent defeat of the Jedi,[[29]](#cite_note-Twilight-29) their Order was declared extinct. Without an enemy to fight, the Inquisitors vanished as well.[[109]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-109) While the exact fate of the organization was unknown to the galaxy at large,[[72]](#cite_note-RiseFall-72) Palpatine had declared that the Inquisitors had outlived their usefulness[[110]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-110) with the defeat of the Jedi,[[109]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-109) raising the possibility that the Inquisitors had been destroyed by their own masters after the Jedi Purge.[[72]](#cite_note-RiseFall-72)

### The rise of Luke Skywalker[]

:   "*That boy is our last hope.*"  
    "*No, there is another.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Yoda, about Luke Skywalker and Leia Organa[[111]](#cite_note-Episode_V-111)

 [![Luke Skywalker began his Jedi training in a time when the Jedi were all but extinct.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/Lukesaberanh.png/revision/latest?cb=20130228054320) [![Luke Skywalker began his Jedi training in a time when the Jedi were all but extinct.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/Lukesaberanh.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130228054320)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/Lukesaberanh.png/revision/latest?cb=20130228054320) 

Luke Skywalker began his Jedi training in a time when the Jedi were all but extinct.

 

Elsewhere in the galaxy, Kenobi and Yoda were also alive.[[112]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-112) Luke Skywalker began his Jedi training under Kenobi, before the Jedi Master was [killed](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia") by Darth Vader.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-12) Skywalker received guidance from Kenobi's spirit, and after a number of years the departed Jedi Master sent Skywalker to Dagobah, where he received more extensive Jedi training from Yoda.[[111]](#cite_note-Episode_V-111)

Skywalker cut his training short in order to rescue his friends [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") and Princess Leia, the latter of whom he did not yet know was his sister, from Vader on [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin "Bespin"). Skywalker soon learned this was a trap, as Vader wanted to capture Skywalker and train him as his new apprentice, and the two engaged in a [lightsaber duel](/wiki/Duel_on_Cloud_City "Duel on Cloud City"). During the duel, Skywalker learned that Vader was his father, and he fled the fight and was rescued by his friends.[[111]](#cite_note-Episode_V-111) A year later, Skywalker proclaimed himself a Jedi Knight and returned to Dagobah, where he found a weary and dying Yoda. Before death, Yoda imparted final wisdom onto his apprentice and confirmed that Vader was his father. He also urged Skywalker to pass on his Jedi training to others. Upon Yoda's death, Skywalker became the last of the Jedi.[[112]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-112)

 [![The deaths of Sidious and Vader marked the end of the Sith lineage, while the Jedi legacy survived through Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/BountyHunters38-VirginVariant-Sprouse.png/revision/latest?cb=20240426002428) [![The deaths of Sidious and Vader marked the end of the Sith lineage, while the Jedi legacy survived through Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/BountyHunters38-VirginVariant-Sprouse.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20240426002428)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ec/BountyHunters38-VirginVariant-Sprouse.png/revision/latest?cb=20240426002428) 

The deaths of Sidious and Vader marked the end of the Sith lineage, while the Jedi legacy survived through Skywalker.

 

Having sensed the goodness in his father, the last vestiges of Anakin Skywalker, Luke surrendered himself to Vader during the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") and was brought before the Emperor. Skywalker and Vader engaged in a final lightsaber duel, and Skywalker nearly turned to the dark side after lashing out at Vader in anger. After defeating his father, Sidious betrayed Vader by ordering Luke to finish him off, but Luke composed himself and tossed [his lightsaber](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker%27s_green_lightsaber "Luke Skywalker's green lightsaber") aside, refusing to fight any further. The furious Emperor attempted to kill Skywalker with his Force lightning, but the sight of his son in agony led to Vader's redemption. Once again Anakin Skywalker, the redeemed Jedi sacrificed himself to kill the Emperor and save his son. Their deaths and the Empire's defeat during the battle ended the era of Sith rule over the galaxy.[[112]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-112)

### Legacy[]

 [![Skywalker's efforts to restore the Jedi Order ended with the deaths of his students.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Jedi_massacre_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20180806000935) [![Skywalker's efforts to restore the Jedi Order ended with the deaths of his students.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Jedi_massacre_TLJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180806000935)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Jedi_massacre_TLJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20180806000935) 

Skywalker's efforts to restore the Jedi Order ended with the deaths of his students.

 

The death of the Emperor, made possible by the return of the Jedi, left the Galactic Empire leaderless. The Empire fractured into competing sects,[[113]](#cite_note-PREVIEWSworldsummary-113) while the Rebel Alliance [reformed](/wiki/Declaration_of_a_New_Republic "Declaration of a New Republic") itself into the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic").[[114]](#cite_note-Aftermath-114) Following the Empire's defeat in the [Battle of Jakku](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku"),[[115]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_New_Edition-115) Sabine Wren and Ahsoka Tano launched a [search](/wiki/Quest_to_find_Ezra_Bridger "Quest to find Ezra Bridger") to find Ezra Bridger, who was still alive,[[116]](#cite_note-Women_of_the_Galaxy-116) and bring him home to Lothal.[[104]](#cite_note-Family&Farewell-104) Author [Ril Shiwer](/wiki/Ril_Shiwer "Ril Shiwer") touched on the Great Jedi Purge in their book *[After Order 66: The Empire's War on the Jedi Order](/wiki/After_Order_66:_The_Empire%27s_War_on_the_Jedi_Order "After Order 66: The Empire's War on the Jedi Order")*, in which Shiwer also pondered why the Empire expended so many resources on hunting an effectively-defeated enemy.[[72]](#cite_note-RiseFall-72)

Heeding Yoda's advice, Luke Skywalker set out to rebuild the Jedi Order and established a [training temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_of_Luke_Skywalker "Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker"). He gathered a group of at least a dozen students which included [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo"), who was the son of Han Solo and Luke's sister, Leia Organa. Skywalker sensed the darkness in his nephew, however, and went to confront him one night. Peering into his nephew's mind, Skywalker saw the terror that his nephew would bring to the galaxy, and in a moment of instinct, ignited his lightsaber. Skywalker quickly came to his senses and was overcome with shame, but Solo woke up and brought down his hut with the Force, collapsing it in on his uncle.[[117]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-117) He then [destroyed the temple](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple") and the Jedi Order[[30]](#cite_note-The_Star_Wars_Book-30) with a storm.[[118]](#cite_note-Kylo_1-118)

Solo had been seduced to the dark side of the Force by the mysterious [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke"), the [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") of the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order"). Solo joined the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren"), taking on the name Kylo Ren, and became Snoke's apprentice. Meanwhile, Skywalker went into self-exile at the [First Jedi Temple](/wiki/First_Jedi_Temple "First Jedi Temple") on [Ahch-To](/wiki/Ahch-To "Ahch-To"),[[119]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-119) only to be brought back into the fold later by the Force-sensitive orphaned [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), who became the last Jedi after Skywalker sacrificed himself at the [Battle of Crait](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait") to save the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance").[[117]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-117)

:   "*The Jedi are a threat to be eradicated wherever they are found.*"
:   ―Fourth Sister[[120]](#cite_note-Realization-120)

Palace").[[122]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-122) * Master [Minas Velti](/wiki/Minas_Velti "Minas Velti"): Killed by troopers of the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion") during the attack on the Jedi Temple.[[27]](#cite_note-Kenobi_I-27) * Master [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"): Killed by Darth Sidious with help from Anakin Skywalker.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) * [Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Huulik](/wiki/Huulik "Huulik"): Died of injuries inflicted by clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") en route to [Rodia](/wiki/Rodia "Rodia").[[123]](#cite_note-Heir_to_the_Jedi-123) * Knight [Sunghi Silpari](/wiki/Sunghi_Silpari "Sunghi Silpari"): Killed by [Clone Captain](/wiki/Clone_Captain "Clone Captain") [Spider](/wiki/Spider_(Clone_Captain) "Spider (Clone Captain)") and members of [Tualon Yaluna's company](/wiki/Tualon_Yaluna%27s_company "Tualon Yaluna's company") during a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Frong "Mission to Frong") to [Frong](/wiki/Frong_(planet) "Frong (planet)").[[20]](#cite_note-Inquisitor:_Rise_of_the_Red_Blade-20) * A [Jedi Temple Guard](/wiki/Unidentified_Jedi_Temple_Guard "Unidentified Jedi Temple Guard"): Killed by Darth Vader during the attack on the Jedi Temple.[[124]](#cite_note-Force_Collector-124) * [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Bene](/wiki/Bene "Bene"): Killed by Darth Vader during the attack on the Jedi Temple.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) * Padawan [Zett Jukassa](/wiki/Zett_Jukassa "Zett Jukassa"): Killed by troopers of the 501st Legion during the attack on the Jedi Temple.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) * Padawan [Whie Malreaux](/wiki/Whie_Malreaux "Whie Malreaux"): Killed by Darth Vader during the attack on the Jedi Temple.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) * Padawan [Marseph](/wiki/Marseph "Marseph"): Initially survived the skirmish on [Zeffo](/wiki/Zeffo "Zeffo") against his clone troopers, but succumbed to his wounds later.[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1) * Youngling [Faris](/wiki/Faris "Faris"): Killed by Darth Vader during the attack on the Jedi Temple.[[26]](#cite_note-Kenobi_IV-26) * Youngling [Katooni](/wiki/Katooni "Katooni"): Presumed to have been killed by Darth Vader during the attack of the Jedi Temple.[[125]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection_31-125) * A [Jedi youngling](/wiki/Unidentified_Jedi_youngling "Unidentified Jedi youngling"): Killed by Darth Vader during the attack on the Jedi Temple.[[5]](#cite_note-Episode_III-5) * A [human Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_Jedi_(Grogu) "Unidentified Jedi (Grogu)"): Killed by troopers of the 501st Legion during the attack on the Jedi Temple.[[126]](#cite_note-The_Mandalorian:_Chapter_20-126) * [Alivar](/wiki/Alivar "Alivar"): Served at an [unidentified location](/wiki/Unidentified_location_(Grandea_and_Alivar) "Unidentified location (Grandea and Alivar)") with Grandea, was executed by their clone troopers after downing several of them.[[79]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_7-79) * [Caladastorous](/wiki/Caladastorous "Caladastorous"): Killed during the fall of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order").[[127]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-127) * [O'ra've](/wiki/O%27ra%27ve "O'ra've"): Killed during the fall of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order").[[127]](#cite_note-Mask_of_Fear-127) * [Palabee](/wiki/Palabee "Palabee"): Killed during the fall of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order").[[77]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_16-77) * Unidentified group of Jedi: Killed by troopers of the 501st Legion during the Massacre on Zondula.[[16]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_4-16)   A few Jedi survived Order 66 and went into hiding. Some succeeded in avoiding the Empire; however, others were tracked down and killed by Vader and the Inquisitorius.   * [Ahmar](/wiki/Ahmar "Ahmar"): Survived Order 66 and was offered the chance to become an Inquisitor. He refused and subsequently tried to break out of the Fortress Inquisitorius. He was killed by the Grand Inquisitor while trying to escape [Nur](/wiki/Nur "Nur").[[128]](#cite_note-Devoted-128) * Master [Kirak Infil'a](/wiki/Kirak_Infil%27a "Kirak Infil'a"): Killed by Darth Vader on the [river](/wiki/Water "Water") [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon") [Al'doleem](/wiki/Al%27doleem "Al'doleem")[[59]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_4-59) in 19 BBY.[[9]](#cite_note-Timelines-9) * [Chief Librarian](/wiki/Chief_Librarian "Chief Librarian") [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu"): Killed by Darth Vader during a [hunt](/wiki/Hunt_for_Jocasta_Nu "Hunt for Jocasta Nu") for her on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") in 19 BBY.[[62]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_10-62) * Master [Luminara Unduli](/wiki/Luminara_Unduli "Luminara Unduli"): Captured and [imprisoned](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner") by the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") at the [Spire](/wiki/Spire_(Stygeon_Prime) "Spire (Stygeon Prime)") on [Stygeon Prime](/wiki/Stygeon_Prime "Stygeon Prime")[[7]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Old_Masters-7) where she was later executed by [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor") between [19](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY") and [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY").[[129]](#cite_note-Luminara-129) * Former Padawan [Ferren Barr](/wiki/Ferren_Barr "Ferren Barr"): Fell to the dark side of the Force[[30]](#cite_note-The_Star_Wars_Book-30) and was killed by Darth Vader on [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala") during the [invasion of Mon Cala](/wiki/Invasion_of_Mon_Cala "Invasion of Mon Cala")[[75]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_17-75) in 18 BBY.[[76]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_16_date-76) * Master [Taron Malicos](/wiki/Taron_Malicos "Taron Malicos"): Survived the initial wave of the Purge when his clone troopers betrayed him. He escaped and crashed his ship on [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir"), where he fell to the dark side of the Force. He was ultimately killed after being buried alive by the [Nightsister](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") [Merrin](/wiki/Merrin "Merrin").[[130]](#cite_note-SWE-130) * A [Zeltron Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_Zeltron_Jedi "Unidentified Zeltron Jedi"): Survived the initial execution of Order 66 during Operation: Knightfall, but was later captured by pirates and imprisoned on the Sith world [Firrhana](/wiki/Firrhana "Firrhana"). Shortly afterwards, she was killed by the Thirteenth Sister.[[20]](#cite_note-Inquisitor:_Rise_of_the_Red_Blade-20) * Knight [Charlin Plaka](/wiki/Charlin_Plaka "Charlin Plaka"): Survived the initial execution of Order 66 during Operation: Knightfall, but was later captured by pirates and imprisoned on the Sith world Firrhana. Shortly afterwards, she was killed by the Thirteenth Sister.[[20]](#cite_note-Inquisitor:_Rise_of_the_Red_Blade-20) * Master [Klefan Opus](/wiki/Klefan_Opus "Klefan Opus"): Survived the initial execution of Order 66 during Operation: Knightfall, but was later captured by pirates and imprisoned on the Sith world Firrhana. Shortly afterwards, he was killed by the [Thirteenth Sister](/wiki/Thirteenth_Sister "Thirteenth Sister").[[20]](#cite_note-Inquisitor:_Rise_of_the_Red_Blade-20) * Former Master [Eeth Koth](/wiki/Eeth_Koth "Eeth Koth"): Killed by Darth Vader on a [desert planet](/wiki/Unidentified_planet_(Eeth_Koth) "Unidentified planet (Eeth Koth)") during a [hunt](/wiki/Hunt_for_Eeth_Koth "Hunt for Eeth Koth") for him in[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2) [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY").[[9]](#cite_note-Timelines-9) * Master [Elan Rast](/wiki/Elan_Rast "Elan Rast"): Killed by the Grand Inquisitor aboard the *[Voyager Dawn](/wiki/Voyager_Dawn "Voyager Dawn")*.[[24]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_1-24)[[131]](#cite_note-Free_Comic_Book_Day_2025:_''Star_Wars''_1-131) * [Pan Delesec](/wiki/Pan_Delesec "Pan Delesec"): Killed by the Grand Inquisitor during a space battle above a planet in the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories").[[16]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_4-16) * [Jed Uhron](/wiki/Jed_Uhron "Jed Uhron"): Killed by the Fifth Brother during a battle in an abandoned [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace").[[16]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_4-16) * Knight [Tensu Run](/wiki/Tensu_Run "Tensu Run"): Killed by Darth Vader on an unidentified planet in the Outer Rim.[[16]](#cite_note-Inquisitors_4-16) * [Velerie Tide](/wiki/Velerie_Tide "Velerie Tide"): Survived the first wave of the purge by blending in with the locals of [Athio III](/wiki/Athio_III "Athio III"). She was later discovered to be a Jedi and was killed by the Inquisitors.[[132]](#cite_note-SDCC_2023_panel-132)[[26]](#cite_note-Kenobi_IV-26) * Knight [Pablo-Jill](/wiki/Pablo-Jill "Pablo-Jill"): Presumed to be alive by the Inquisitorius. Later found entombed in the Fortress Inquisitorius by 9 BBY.[[133]](#cite_note-Death-133) * Master [Tera Sinube](/wiki/Tera_Sinube "Tera Sinube"): Presumed to be alive by the Inquisitorius. Later found entombed in the Fortress Inquisitorius by 9 BBY.[[26]](#cite_note-Kenobi_IV-26)[[134]](#cite_note-Tera_tweet-134) * [Nari](/wiki/Nari "Nari"): Killed by the Inquisitorius on Tatooine.[[27]](#cite_note-Kenobi_I-27) * Former Knight [Dagan Gera](/wiki/Dagan_Gera "Dagan Gera"): Survived by being in a stasis tank on [Koboh](/wiki/Koboh "Koboh") from the era of the High Republic until the rise of the Empire. Awakened from his slumber by Cal Kestis, and later killed by Kestis in [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY").[[135]](#cite_note-Jedi_Survivor-135) * Master [Eno Cordova](/wiki/Eno_Cordova "Eno Cordova"): Initially survived the purge by hiding in the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions"), he later reunited with his old padawan and formed a new Jedi cache with her. He was later killed by Bode Akuna on [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha") in [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY").[[135]](#cite_note-Jedi_Survivor-135) * Master [Cere Junda](/wiki/Cere_Junda "Cere Junda"): Originally a Jedi Knight, survived the initial wave from her clone troopers but was captured by the Galactic Empire and imprisoned and tortured. She later escaped and forfeited her Jedi identity. She later founded a secret Jedi cache on Jedha alongside her master. She was killed by Darth Vader on Jedha.[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1)[[135]](#cite_note-Jedi_Survivor-135) * Former Knight [Bode Akuna](/wiki/Bode_Akuna "Bode Akuna"): Survived the initial purge and went into hiding. He later met a woman with whom he had a daughter, [Kata](/wiki/Kata_Akuna "Kata Akuna"). He later fell to the dark side and brokered a deal with ISB officer [Denvik](/wiki/Lank_Denvik "Lank Denvik") to keep him and his daughter safe from Inquisitors as long as Bode served as an Imperial spy. He was killed by Cal Kestis on [Tanalorr](/wiki/Tanalorr "Tanalorr").[[135]](#cite_note-Jedi_Survivor-135) * [Zubain Ankonori](/wiki/Zubain_Ankonori "Zubain Ankonori"): Killed by an Inquisitor on [Mataou](/wiki/Mataou "Mataou").[[136]](#cite_note-Uprising-136) * [Khandra](/wiki/Khandra "Khandra"): Killed by an Inquisitor on [Burnin Konn](/wiki/Burnin_Konn "Burnin Konn").[[136]](#cite_note-Uprising-136) * [Mususiel](/wiki/Mususiel "Mususiel"): Killed by an [Inquisitor](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius") on [Anoat](/wiki/Anoat "Anoat").[[136]](#cite_note-Uprising-136) * [Nuhj](/wiki/Nuhj "Nuhj"): Killed by an Inquisitor on Burnin Konn.[[136]](#cite_note-Uprising-136) * An [Unidentified Jedi](/wiki/Jod_Na_Nawood%27s_master "Jod Na Nawood's master"): Survived Order 66 and briefly trained [Jod Na Nawood](/wiki/Jod_Na_Nawood "Jod Na Nawood") in the ways of the Force, but was found and killed.[[69]](#cite_note-SC6-69)   Members of the Inquisitorius killed during the Purge:   * [Dante](/wiki/Dante "Dante"): Survived Order 66 and was given the chance to become an Inquisitor. He was killed by Barriss Offee during their trial to become Inquisitors.[[128]](#cite_note-Devoted-128) * Former Padawan [Heezo](/wiki/Heezo "Heezo"): Once a Padawan of the Jedi Order, Heezo failed the [Jedi Trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials") and was reassigned as a Temple staff technician by the [Council of Reassignment](/wiki/Council_of_Reassignment "Council of Reassignment") of the Jedi Order. Growing dissatisfied and tired of the [Jedi Council](/wiki/Jedi_Council "Jedi Council"), Heezo secretly became a spy for Darth Sidious inside the Jedi Temple, helping turn other Jedi to the Dark Side. Later on, he managed to survive Order 66 and became an agent of the Inquisitorius operating on their [headquarters](/wiki/Inquisitorius_Headquarters "Inquisitorius Headquarters") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"). He was killed a few months later by the newly appointed Thirteenth Sister.[[20]](#cite_note-Inquisitor:_Rise_of_the_Red_Blade-20) * Master [Prosset Dibs](/wiki/Tenth_Brother "Tenth Brother"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitorius, although he had already shown a rebellious attitude towards the Jedi Order prior to his descent to the Dark Side. He was killed by [Purge Troopers](/wiki/Purge_Trooper "Purge Trooper") that had their inhibitor chips activated by fugitive Padawan Ferren Barr while being chased by the Inquisitors and Vader on Mon Cala.[[75]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_17-75) * [Bil Valen](/wiki/Sixth_Brother "Sixth Brother"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitorius. He was defeated and killed one year after the purge by Ahsoka Tano on the moon [Raada](/wiki/Raada "Raada").[[22]](#cite_note-Ahsoka-22) * [Eleventh Brother](/wiki/Eleventh_Brother "Eleventh Brother"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitorius, although he was later killed by Ahsoka.[[23]](#cite_note-Resolve-23)[[137]](#cite_note-Resolve_date-137) * [An unidentified Inquistor](/wiki/Unidentified_Inquisitor_(Asajj_Ventress) "Unidentified Inquisitor (Asajj Ventress)") conducted a [hunt](/wiki/Hunt_for_Lyco_Strata "Hunt for Lyco Strata") for the Padawan Lyco Strata. While hunting for the boy, he encountered the former [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice") [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress") with whom he dueled until he was stabbed in the back by Strata, killing him.[[138]](#cite_note-A_Way_Forward-138) * Knight [Iskat Akaris](/wiki/Thirteenth_Sister "Thirteenth Sister"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitorius, becoming the Thirteenth Sister. She was killed by Darth Vader in [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY").[[20]](#cite_note-Inquisitor:_Rise_of_the_Red_Blade-20)[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2) * Knight [Tualon Yaluna](/wiki/Tualon_Yaluna "Tualon Yaluna"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitorius. He was killed by Darth Vader in [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY").[[20]](#cite_note-Inquisitor:_Rise_of_the_Red_Blade-20)[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2) * Padawan [Trilla Suduri](/wiki/Second_Sister "Second Sister"): Survived until she was discovered by the Empire and turned into an Inquisitor. She was later killed by Darth Vader during the [mission to Nur](/wiki/Mission_to_Nur "Mission to Nur") in[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1) [14 BBY](/wiki/14_BBY "14 BBY").[[80]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order_date-80) * Knight [Masana Tide](/wiki/Ninth_Sister "Ninth Sister"): Survived Order 66 and was locked away in isolation until she finally surrendered to the Dark Side and joined the Inquisitorius. She was killed by Cal Kestis on Coruscant in [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY").[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1)[[135]](#cite_note-Jedi_Survivor-135) * [An unidentified Inquisitor](/wiki/Jerserra%27s_master "Jerserra's master") became the master of Jerserra whilst on Dathomir. She was killed by her apprentice between [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY") and [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY "5 ABY").[[139]](#cite_note-Ghosts_of_Dathomir-139)[[140]](#cite_note-Jerserra's_master's_death-140)   **The following section contains information from *[Star Wars: Visions](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Visions "Star Wars: Visions")* media that was referenced in no other [canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") source. [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm") has stated that *Visions* stories and their related media are not required to "tie into the larger chronology" of *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* storytelling. Editor discretion is advised.**   * [An Inquisitor](/wiki/Unidentified_Inquisitor_(T0-B1) "Unidentified Inquisitor (T0-B1)") was killed by [T0-B1](/wiki/T0-B1 "T0-B1") and [C03](/wiki/C03 "C03") sometime during the Great Jedi Purge.[[141]](#cite_note-T0-B1-141) * [An Inquisitor](/wiki/Unidentified_Inquisitor_(Golak) "Unidentified Inquisitor (Golak)") was killed by [Rugal](/wiki/Rugal "Rugal") sometime during the Great Jedi Purge.[[142]](#cite_note-Golak-142)   ***Star Wars: Visions* information ends here.**   * Former Knight and Jedi Temple Guard [The Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitorius. He was later killed by Kanan Jarrus during the [Action at Mustafar](/wiki/Action_at_Mustafar "Action at Mustafar").[[115]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_New_Edition-115) * [Seventh Sister](/wiki/Seventh_Sister "Seventh Sister"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitrious after the [Empire's founding](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order"). She was later killed by Maul during the Mission to Malachor.[[115]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_New_Edition-115) * [Fifth Brother](/wiki/Fifth_Brother "Fifth Brother"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitorius. He was later killed by [Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul") during the [Mission to Malachor](/wiki/Mission_to_Malachor "Mission to Malachor").[[115]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_New_Edition-115) * [Eighth Brother](/wiki/Eighth_Brother "Eighth Brother"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitrious after the [Empire's founding](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order"). He was later killed during the Mission to Malachor.[[115]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars_New_Edition-115) |

## Known survivors[]

:   "*I... I might be one of the last of my kind.*"
:   ―Cal Kestis[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1)

Several Jedi or former Jedi eluded capture or death during the Purge and survived, though several were killed after its conclusion.

* Grand Master [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda"): Survived in exile on [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah") until his death in [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY").[[112]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-112)
* Master [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"): Survived until his death on the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") during the [Rescue of Princess Leia](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia")[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-12) in [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY").[[143]](#cite_note-IV_Date-143)
* Master [Vanzell Mar-Klar](/wiki/Vanzell_Mar-Klar "Vanzell Mar-Klar"): Survived the Great Jedi Purge alongside Nedriss Narr and two other padawans. They dedicated the rest of their days into finding and training future [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight").[[144]](#cite_note-Trials-144)
* Knight [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus"): Initially a Padawan, survived until being killed on [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal") during the [rescue of Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Rescue_of_Hera_Syndulla_(Lothal) "Rescue of Hera Syndulla (Lothal)")[[106]](#cite_note-Jedi_Night-106) [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY").[[145]](#cite_note-Chronology_Note_Heroes_of_Mandalore-145)
* Padawan [Nedriss Narr](/wiki/Nedriss_Narr "Nedriss Narr"): Survived the Great Jedi Purge alongside Vanzell Mar-Klar and two other padawans. They dedicated the rest of their days into finding and training future Jedi Knights.[[144]](#cite_note-Trials-144)
* Former Knight [Baylan Skoll](/wiki/Baylan_Skoll "Baylan Skoll"): Survived the Great Jedi Purge and became a mercenary. During the [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era"), he operated along with his apprentice [Shin Hati](/wiki/Shin_Hati "Shin Hati").[[146]](#cite_note-Empire-146)
* Former Knight [Grandea](/wiki/Grandea "Grandea"): Survived the Great Jedi Purge by leaving the Jedi way behind. She encountered [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") in [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY").[[79]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_7-79)
* Former Padawan [Naq Med](/wiki/Naq_Med "Naq Med"): Survived until his death during the [New Republic Era](/wiki/New_Republic_Era "New Republic Era").[[124]](#cite_note-Force_Collector-124)
* Former Padawan [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"): Survived after a [skirmish](/wiki/Skirmish_aboard_the_Tribunal "Skirmish aboard the Tribunal") aboard the *[Tribunal](/wiki/Tribunal "Tribunal")* against the 501st [Legion](/wiki/Legion "Legion") and [Coruscant Guard](/wiki/Coruscant_Guard "Coruscant Guard").[[15]](#cite_note-Shattered-15)
* Former Youngling [Din Grogu](/wiki/Din_Grogu "Din Grogu"): Survived Operation: Knightfall and the Great Jedi Purge by being taken into hiding.[[49]](#cite_note-The_Mandalorian:_Chapter_13-49)
* [Mill Alibeth](/wiki/Mill_Alibeth "Mill Alibeth"): Survived Order 66 and lived through the [First Order-Resistance War](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War") as a bounty hunter alongside fellow initiate Vivert Stag.[[147]](#cite_note-HS_4-147)
* [Vivert Stag](/wiki/Vivert_Stag "Vivert Stag"): Survived Order 66 and lived through the First Order-Resistance War as a bounty hunter alongside fellow initiate Mill Alibeth.[[147]](#cite_note-HS_4-147)
* [Kira Vantala](/wiki/Kira_Vantala "Kira Vantala"): According to legend, survived the Great Jedi Purge and encountered and dueled with [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor") on [Gaaten](/wiki/Gaaten "Gaaten").[[148]](#cite_note-Orphanage-148)

## Order 66 survivors with unknown fates[]

|  |
| --- |
| Many Jedi survived Order 66, however, it is unknown if they survived the entirety of the Purge until its end in [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY").   * Master [Kelleran Beq](/wiki/Kelleran_Beq "Kelleran Beq"): Survived Operation: Knightfall with the help of the [Royal Naboo Security Forces](/wiki/Royal_Naboo_Security_Forces "Royal Naboo Security Forces") and fled Coruscant with Grogu.[[126]](#cite_note-The_Mandalorian:_Chapter_20-126) * Master [Coleman Kcaj](/wiki/Coleman_Kcaj "Coleman Kcaj"): Presumed to be alive by the Inquisitorius.[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2) * Master [Oppo Rancisis](/wiki/Oppo_Rancisis "Oppo Rancisis"): Presumed to be alive by the Inquisitorius.[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2) * Master [Uvell](/wiki/Uvell "Uvell"): Survived the first wave of the Purge.[[149]](#cite_note-End_of_History-149) * Master [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos"): Survived and started the [Hidden Path](/wiki/Hidden_Path "Hidden Path") to help smuggle Force-sensitive younglings and Jedi into safety from the Empire.[[32]](#cite_note-Kenobi_III-32) * Knight [Cal Kestis](/wiki/Cal_Kestis "Cal Kestis"): Initially a Padawan, survived the skirmish above [Bracca](/wiki/Bracca "Bracca") against the 13th [Battalion](/wiki/Battalion "Battalion") before being found by fellow Knight Cere Junda and chased by the Second Sister and the Ninth Sister.[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1) * Padawan [Gungi](/wiki/Gungi "Gungi"): Survived Order 66, but was later captured by the [Vanguard Axis](/wiki/Vanguard_Axis "Vanguard Axis") while trying to get back to [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"). He was later aided by [Clone Force 99](/wiki/Clone_Force_99 "Clone Force 99") in his quest to reach, settle on, and protect his homeworld.[[150]](#cite_note-Tribe-150) * Padawan [Lyco Strata](/wiki/Lyco_Strata "Lyco Strata"): Survived Order 66 and tried to hide from the Empire by finding the [Hidden Path](/wiki/Hidden_Path "Hidden Path"). During his search for them, he encountered Asajj Ventress, who offered to help him find the Path. After obtain intel on the Hidden Path's location, Lyco and Ventress finally found a safehouse of the Path located in [Cipher Canyon](/wiki/Cipher_Canyon "Cipher Canyon"). However, he instead chose to remain with Ventress instead of going with the Path.[[138]](#cite_note-A_Way_Forward-138)[[151]](#cite_note-One_Warrior_to_Another-151) * Youngling [Reva Sevander](/wiki/Reva_Sevander "Reva Sevander"): Survived the Siege on the Jedi Temple and joined the Inquisitorius. She would later abandon her life as an Inquisitor in search of solace.[[25]](#cite_note-Kenobi_V-25)[[83]](#cite_note-Kenobi_VI-83) * Former Knight [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee"): Survived Order 66 by being imprisoned in the [Imperial Inspectorate HQ](/wiki/Imperial_Inspectorate_HQ "Imperial Inspectorate HQ") for crimes against the Republic. She briefly joined the Inquisitorius, before she quit after a mission and became a healer. She was hunted down and fatally wounded by the Fourth Sister, before she helped Barriss out of the cave they were fighting in by carrying her out.[[152]](#cite_note-The_Way_Out-152) * A [human Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_human_Jedi "Unidentified human Jedi"): Survived Order 66 and was hunted down by the Fourth Sister and Barriss Offee. In the end, Offee betrayed the Inquisitorius and helped the Jedi live.[[120]](#cite_note-Realization-120) * [A Rodian Jedi youngling](/wiki/Unidentified_Rodian_Jedi_youngling "Unidentified Rodian Jedi youngling"): Survived in hiding with Cere Junda and Trilla Suduri.[[1]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-1) * [Selrahc Eluos](/wiki/Selrahc_Eluos "Selrahc Eluos"): Presumed to be alive by the Inquisitorius.[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2) * [Ka-Moon Kholi](/wiki/Ka-Moon_Kholi "Ka-Moon Kholi"): Presumed to be alive by the Inquisitorius.[[2]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_19-2) * [Lyn Rakish](/wiki/Fourth_Sister "Fourth Sister"): Survived Order 66 and joined the Inquisitorius. She later redeemed herself after stabbing Barriss Offee and aiding her afterwards, abandoning her life as an Inquisitor.[[84]](#cite_note-Part_II-84)[[152]](#cite_note-The_Way_Out-152) |

## Behind the scenes[]

In the [LEGO](/wiki/LEGO "LEGO") comic "[Ambush in the Temple](/wiki/The_Temple_Ambush "The Temple Ambush")," two Padawan survivors—[Nena Gallow](/wiki/Nena_Gallow "Nena Gallow") and [Mel Acan](/wiki/Mel_Acan "Mel Acan")—are featured. Both lost their masters to the Jedi Purge. While both were hiding out in a [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_(Vinee) "Jedi Temple (Vinee)") on [Vinee](/wiki/Vinee "Vinee"), they are discovered by the Grand Inquisitor and Darth Vader, but both Padawans escape.[[153]](#cite_note-Temple_Ambush-153) The LEGO comic "[The Special Suits](/wiki/The_Special_Suits "The Special Suits")" sees stormtrooper [TK-101](/wiki/TK-101 "TK-101") claim Vader hunted down a surviving Jedi named [Tanga Wattal](/wiki/Tanga_Wattal "Tanga Wattal"), only for Vader himself to say he did not remember that happening.[[154]](#cite_note-Special_Suits-154)

**The following section contains information from *[Star Wars: Visions](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Visions "Star Wars: Visions")* media that was referenced in no other [canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") source. [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm") has stated that *Visions* stories and their related media are not required to "tie into the larger chronology" of *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* storytelling. Editor discretion is advised.**

In the *[Star Wars: Visions](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Visions "Star Wars: Visions")* short film "[Tatooine Rhapsody](/wiki/Tatooine_Rhapsody "Tatooine Rhapsody")," the character [Jay](/wiki/Jee_Ken_Tsokee "Jee Ken Tsokee") survived Order 66, and hid by joining a band called [Star Waver](/wiki/Star_Waver "Star Waver").[[155]](#cite_note-Tatooine_Rhapsody-155) A survivor known only as "[F](/wiki/F "F")" is featured in the short "[The Village Bride](/wiki/The_Village_Bride "The Village Bride")."[[156]](#cite_note-Village_Bride-156)

***Star Wars: Visions* information ends here.**

[↑](#cite_ref-Death_133-0) [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") [Part IV Episode Guide | Obi-Wan Kenobi](https://www.starwars.com/series/obi-wan-kenobi/part-iv-guide) on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220805052203/https://www.starwars.com/series/obi-wan-kenobi/part-iv-guide)) establishes that Pablo-Jill was [killed](/wiki/Death "Death") between [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") and the events of *[Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Star Wars: Obi-Wan Kenobi")* "[Part IV](/wiki/Part_IV "Part IV")," which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY") and [9 BBY](/wiki/9_BBY "9 BBY"), respectively. 134. [↑](#cite_ref-Tera_tweet_134-0) [TwitterLogo](https://twitter.com) [Star Wars](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm") ([@starwars](https://twitter.com/starwars)) on [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "wikipedia:Twitter") ([post](https://twitter.com/starwars/status/705515259373723649)): "@sskyguyy We had to commemorate a fallen Jedi Master💔" ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20220613172810/https://twitter.com/starwars/status/705515259373723649)) 135. ↑ [135.0](#cite_ref-Jedi_Survivor_135-0) [135.1](#cite_ref-Jedi_Survivor_135-1) [135.2](#cite_ref-Jedi_Survivor_135-2) [135.3](#cite_ref-Jedi_Survivor_135-3) [135.4](#cite_ref-Jedi_Survivor_135-4) *[Star Wars Jedi: Survivor](/wiki/Star_Wars_Jedi:_Survivor "Star Wars Jedi: Survivor")* 136. ↑ [136.0](#cite_ref-Uprising_136-0) [136.1](#cite_ref-Uprising_136-1) [136.2](#cite_ref-Uprising_136-2) [136.3](#cite_ref-Uprising_136-3) *[Star Wars: Uprising](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Uprising "Star Wars: Uprising")* 137. [↑](#cite_ref-Resolve_date_137-0) [*Ahsoka*](/wiki/Ahsoka_(novel) "Ahsoka (novel)") establishes that the [Sixth Brother](/wiki/Sixth_Brother "Sixth Brother") was the first [Inquisitor](/wiki/Inquisitor "Inquisitor") [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") ever encountered. *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of *Ahsoka* to [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"). As such, the main events of "[Resolve](/wiki/Resolve_(episode) "Resolve (episode)")" must take place during or after that year because it features Tano [encountering](/wiki/Attack_on_a_farm_village "Attack on a farm village") a different [Inquisitor](/wiki/Eleventh_Brother "Eleventh Brother"). It also takes place before Tano actively became part of the Rebellion by the events of "[Out of Darkness](/wiki/Out_of_Darkness "Out of Darkness")," which *Timelines* dates to [5 BBY](/wiki/5_BBY "5 BBY"). 138. ↑ [138.0](#cite_ref-A_Way_Forward_138-0) [138.1](#cite_ref-A_Way_Forward_138-1) [TalesoftheUnderworld-Logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Underworld "Star Wars: Tales of the Underworld") *[Star Wars: Tales of the Underworld](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Underworld "Star Wars: Tales of the Underworld")* — "[A Way Forward](/wiki/A_Way_Forward "A Way Forward")" 139. [↑](#cite_ref-Ghosts_of_Dathomir_139-0) *[Ghosts of Dathomir](/wiki/Ghosts_of_Dathomir "Ghosts of Dathomir")* 140. [↑](#cite_ref-Jerserra's_master's_death_140-0) Jerserra's master discovered Jerserra plural "[years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year")" (meaning more than one year) after the [Battle of Dathomir](/wiki/Battle_of_Dathomir "Battle of Dathomir"), which took place in [20 BBY](/wiki/20_BBY "20 BBY"), as stated in *[Ghosts of Dathomir](/wiki/Ghosts_of_Dathomir "Ghosts of Dathomir")*. Therefore, the events occurred during or after 18 BBY, two years after. We also know that the events of *Ghosts of Dathomir* took place during the reign of the Empire, as stated as much, so before or during 5 ABY. 141. [↑](#cite_ref-T0-B1_141-0) [Star-Wars-Visions-series-logo-short](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Visions "Star Wars: Visions") *[Star Wars: Visions](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Visions "Star Wars: Visions")* — "[T0-B1](/wiki/T0-B1_(short_film) "T0-B1 (short film)")" 142.
